greateſt offyces dignytyes ye cyuyle cōmunyties ſoeuer parte taken ſeuerallye ſelfe agayne thoughe graunte trewe deade ſome vnlerned men ſo wel iudge lawe agyble thynge whiche inſtytuted ordayned ſo many learned men yet nōbre vnlerned men myght made ſo great beynge ſo great multytude myght iudge euen well theſe thynges ye euen vnlerned men alſo may dyſcerne lawes made elles better lerned men beynge fewe nombre aryſtotle ſayd ſame place afore alledged wyllynge confyrme ſtrength fortyfye ſentence yf multytude ſay aryſtotle ouer dull ygnorante ſeruyle albeit eche one hym ſelfe iudge ſo well ben lerned wyſe hathe knowledge yet togyther ſhall iudge better leaſt wyſe worſe auctoryte howe auctorite ſtultorum infinitus eſt munerus taken vnderſtanded taken fyrſte chapytre eccleſiaſtes nombre fooles infynyte ought ſaye worde ſtultorum engliſſhe fooles vnderſtanded vnlearned men gyueth theyr mynde lyberal workes whiche hath vnderſtandynge iudgement thynges done thoughe ſo moche whiche gyue theyr mynde ſuche thynges elles perauenture fooles place whiche man ſygnyfyed meaned infydels ſaynt iherome vpon place whiche infydels myſcreantes ye haue neuer ſo moche cūnynge knowlege worldely ſcyences yet ſtarke fooles accordynge ſayenge ſaynt paule thyrde chapytre ye fyrſt epyſtle ye coryntheans ye wyſdome world foolyſſhnes afore god ſecōde obieccyon ſmal ſtrēgth albeit yt eaſy fewe men agre one ſentence mynde many yet hereof concluded ſentence fewe parte better ſentence hoole multitude wherof ye ſayd fewe porcyon parte theſe fewe coulde ne wolde ſo well dyſcerne iudge cōmune profyte coulde wolde hole multytude cytezens ye moreouer ieopardouſe hath appered thynges aforeſayde cōmytte makynge lawe arbytrement iudgement fewe men perauenture makynge lawe wolde haue reſpecte partyculer profyte ſome perſones ſome company cōmune profyte thynge appereth euydently maker ye decretals reſpecte togyther owne ſynguſer profyte whiche maker decretalles clerkes clergye ſhall ſhewe alſo suffycyentlye viii chapytre ſeconde dyccyon hereof ſhulde begyuen certayne occaſyon waye opened regyment called olygarchia lykewyſe whan powre makynge lawes graunted one man alone occaſyon gyuen tyranny haue brought alledged heretofore xi chapytre aryſtotle v etykes treatyſe de iuſticia thyrde obieccyon maye eaſely put anſwered vnto thoſe oligarchia declared fore ye viii chapytre thynges whiche hath ben ſayd redye albeit wyſe men lawes may better made vnlerned men yet concluded hereof lawes better made onely wyſe men hole multytude cytezens whiche multytude aforeſayde wyſe men alſo included hole multytude theſe gathered togyther myght wolde better dycerne cōmune vtylyte profyte cōmune iuſtyce theſe partes taken ſeuerallye ſelues yea thoughe neuer ſo great wyſe men wherfore ſay trewe ſoeuer ſayth vnlerned multytude doth hynder let eleccyon apporbacyon truth cōmune profyte good rather great helpe thynge whan ioyned cūnynge whiche hathe experyence albeit ſelues theyr owne wyttes inuente fynde true thynges profytable thynges whiche inſtytuted ordayned yet maye dyſcerne iudge ſayd thynges beynge inuented men purpoſed moued vnto whether yf thynge ſeme added mynyſſhed vtterlye chaunged dyſpyſed refuſed ſayd thynges put moued man perceyueth many thynges alſo may helpe fynyſſhynge makynge perfyte many thynges hathe harde man ſpeake begynnynge inuē cyon whiche thynges coulde haue come hym ſelfe owne wyt alone inuencyon fyrſte fyndynge thynges harde wherfore aryſtotle ſaythe ſeconde boke eleuches laſt chapytre harde thynge fynde fyrſt begynnynge trouth begynnīges thynges harde founde maner dyſcyplyne ſcyēce ye begynnīge beyng one foūde eaſy thynge adde put reſydue wherfore fynde begynnynges pryncyples ſcyences artes tradycyons appertayneth vnto men beſt moſte ſharpe wyttes thoſe thynges whiche inuented redy men courſe groſſe wyt may adde called herfore vndyſcrete fooles becauſe inuēte fynde ſuche thynges ſelues theyr owne wyttes rather ought accompted nombre good men ſayde aryſtotle fyrſt etykes iiii chapytre man beſt whiche knoweth thynges mā beſt hym ſelfe koweth thynges done hym ſelfe nedeth teachynge agayne good man dothe obeye hym ſayth well gyueth hym good counſayle ſay whiche harkeneth hym dothe ſaye agaynſt hym without reaſon cauſe therfore conuenyent profytable cōmytted wyſe experte men hole multytude cytezens ſerche fynde examyne rule cōmune cyuyle iuſtyce vtylytes dyſprofytes ſuche lyke thynges whiche rule made lawes ſtatutes ſo ſuche maner outher euery one pryncypall partes cyuyle cōmunyte reakened vp v chapytre dyccyon fyrſte parte therof certayne elected choſen yet accordynge proporcyon euery one thoſe partes elles cytezens gathered togyther aforeſayd experte wyſe men elected ſhal conuenyent profytable maner aſſemblynge cōmynge togyther inuentynge maner inuentyng fyndynge lawes deuyſynge lawes without noyaunce harme multytude wyt vnlearned leſſe wyſe men whiche ſhulde lytle helpe furtheraunce ſerchynge ſuche maner rule lawes ſhulde troubled letted theyr owne workes neceſſarye occupacyons whiche thynge ſhulde chargeable paynefull bothe eche one ſeuerally alſo cōmune ſuche rule beynge inuented dylygently examyned made lawes ought put forth approued reproued alowed dyſalowed amonge hole multytude cyuyle cōmunyte beynge congregated aſſembled togyther yf cōmunes ſhall ſeme thynge ought added mynyſſhed taken awaye chaunged vtterly deſpyſed refuſed maye tell ſhewe mynde reaſon hereof lawe maye profytably inſtytuted made haue aforeſayde cytezens whiche leſſe learned wyſe maye otherwhyles perceyue ſomwhat amended aboute lawe purpoſed whiche coulde haue inuented founde lawe becauſe lawes gyuen iudgment conſente hole vnyuerſall multytude ſhall better obſerued kepte neyther man ſhall haue cauſe ſpeake el grudge agaynſt ſayde rule whiche made lawes publyſſhed openly declared amonge hole vnyuerſall cōgregacyon cytezens whiche wolde ſpeake ſaye thynge reaſonably concernynge ſayd rule haue ben harde ſpeake ſaye theyr myndes ought agayne choſen ſuche maner men maner haue aforeſayde elles aforeſayde men confyrmed whiche repreſentynge ye ſtede auctoryte ye hole multytude cytezēs ſhal apꝓue dyſalowe ye aforeſayde rule ſought forth purpoſed hole ye parte el ye hole multitude cytezēs togyther ye bygger parte ſhal ye ſame yf lyſt whiche approbacyon made ſayde rule lawes worthy ſo called theſe alſo onely humayne preceptes publycacion proclamacyon oblygate bynde tranſgreſſours cyuyle offence blame cyuyle paine whan lawes dothe bynde auctoryte makynge inſtytucyon lawes gyue coactyue precepte obſeruacyon dothe appertayne belonge onely hole multytude cytezēs bygger parte therof effectyue cauſe hym whiche whome ſayde generall multytude ſhall graunt auctoryte thynke haue ſuffycyently declared ſhewed thynges nowe aforeſayd ¶ qualytes dyſpoſycyons property belongynge perfyte gouernour y• ende yt maye knowen maner perſone prynce gouernour ought qualyte wherof alſo appereth conuenyent mater ſubiecte call lawes man xiiii chapytre premyſſes entende breyfelie declare maner perſone ought whiche ſhulde beare offyce gouernour ii intrinſecall habytes qualytes propertyes belongynge hym ſhall perfyte gouernoure whiche qualyties ſhal price gouernour ought haue hym ii qualytes departed dyſſeuered one wyt prudence morall vertue namely iuſtyce ryghtuouſnes one wyt prudence neceſſarie ende mynde vnderſtandynge hym may dyrected gouernynge exercyſynge offyce wherfore aryſtotle thyrde boke thyrde chapytre polytykes ſayth thus prudence alone propre vertue ruler gouernour touchynge vertues ſeme cōmune well ſubiectes ruler gouernours ſeconde qualyte habyte neceſſarie ende affeccyon may ryght wyt morall vertue pryncypally amonge al iuſtyce ryghtuouſnes wherfore v boke etikes vi chapytre aryſtotle ſaythe thus heed offycer prynce gouernour keper maynteyner defēder iuſtyce ryght wherfore conclude prudence neceſſary hym ſhall gouernoure maye dyrected well propre worke propre worke prynce gouernoure wyt iudgementes cyuyle ryghtes vtylyties theſe cyuyle actes wherin acte ſelfe maner determyned lawe prynce iudge dyrected prudence iudgynge alſo doynge execucyon acte maner bothe myght chaunce happen hym myſſe without wyſdome prudence red saluſte catifine complices ponyſſhed cicero hyſtorye batayle catilyne made agaynſt romayns cicero whiche tyme conſull ponyſſhed complyces catiline beynge cytezens rome noble myghty men whiche conſpyred agaynſt cōmune welthe therfore worthye deathe yf ſaye ponyſſhed accordynge law ſame place tyme place tyme ordre execucyon may ſome ſeaſō vpon good polycye altered ſame maner ordre afore dayes vſed cuſtomed lykely hod wolde haue ryſen reaſon therof cyuyle batayle amonge theyr owne ſelues whiche ſhulde haue dyſtroyed cōmune weale ſuche ſedycyonreyſed ſtyred vp people theſe ſayd conſpyrers traytours agaynſt counſayles heed offycers ruler ieopardie cicero conſull one ii chefe ruler heed offycers cytie eſcaped auoyded wyſdome prudence whan delyuered ſayde malefactours wyſdome cicero tullianum yt execuſyon hangman cōmaunded kylled place pryſon whiche perauenture therfore called tullianum wyſdome counſayles purpoſes maners agyble thynges dyrected wherfore aryſtotle vi boke etikes v chapytre ſayth thus prudencia eſt habitus verus cum ratione actibus circa hominis bona vel deſcrypcyon prudence mala prudēce practyue habyte qualytie man worketh true reaſon touchynge thoſe thynges whiche good euyll man vnderſtande thou man cauſe hereof thoſe agyble thynges aboute whiche moſt parte lawes made accordynge whiche lawes prynce gouernoure ought dyſpoſe ordre cyuyle actes men becauſe ſemeth poſſyble alwayes determyne lawe maners cyrcumſtances whiche may happen aboute doynge ſayde actes reaſon great varyetye dyuerſyte accordynge dyuerſyte regyons tymes open experyence teacheth alſo aryſtotle wytneſſeth fyrſt boke etikes thyrde chapytre whan ſaythe wyſe honeſt thynges ryghtuouſe thynges wherof morall philoſopher maketh conſyderacyon hathe ſo great dyfference errour maye ſeme ſuche onely lawe nature ſaye onely becauſe men wyll ſo ſtatute ordayne becauſe nature agyble thynges determynate wyt thynge ryght thynge wronge expreſſeth ſame largely thyrde boke polytykes xii chapitre whan ſayth thus becauſe certayne thynges may cōprehended lawes certayne may therfore aſke queſtyon make doubte whether better gouerned beſte man beſte lawes vnpoſſyble lawe maye gyuen thoſe ſame thynges vnderſtande thou thoſe thynges whiche may mater conſultacyon wherof men may take counſayle togyther therfore neceſſary cōmytte iudgment ſome certayne doubtfull thynges whiche dothe happen chaunce cyuyle actes men vnto arbytrement deſcrecyon prynces iudges wyt ſuche thynges whiche outher touchyuge ſelues touchynge ſome maner cyrcumſtaunce determyned lawe ſuche thynges determyned lawe prynce gonernoure ought prynce gouernour ought folowe ye lawe folowe determynacyon lawe mynde ſentence aryſtotle thyrde boke polytykes vii chapytre whan ſayd wyſe prynces gouernours whether one el mo one gouerneth ruleth ought haue powre auctoryte thoſe thynges wherof lawes ſuffycyently exactlye ſpeake make mencyon expreſſely becauſe harde thynge generall ſpeche ſuche law cōprehende euery partyculer caſe maye happen whiche ſentence reherſynge agayne xii chapytre ſame boke ſayth thus alſo nowe gouernours heed offycers whiche haue powre iudge ſome certayne thynges without lawe ſuche thynges wherof lawe determyne iudge gouernoure ſhall gyue iudgement yf lawe couldenot haue gyuen precepte well ſayd thyngꝭ ſuch thynges wherof lawe maye determyne man wolde doubte prudence therfore neceſſary prudence neceſſary prynce prynce gouernoure iudgynge ſuche maner thynges whiche determyned lawe ſentence aryſtotle beynge nere pryncyples whiche euydent ſelues ſoeuer lyſte may certyfie demonſtratyue ſillogiſme reaſon thoſe thynges whiche hath ben ſayde ſeconde chapytre dyccyon agayne morall goodnes vertue prynce ought iuſte ryght tuouſe ſpecyally iuſtyce ryghtuouſnes neceſſary prynce gouernour yf peruerſe euyll perſone touchynge maners cōmune weale cyuyle gouernaunce greatly hurte hym neuer ſo well inſtructed appoynted lawes haue ſayde harde poſſyble determyne maner caſes maye happen lawes ſome thynges muſt nedes cōmytted arbytrement wyll prynce gouernoure whiche thynge maye hurte cōmune weale yf man peruerſe affeccyon ſentence mynde aryſtotle ſeconde boke politikes viii chapytre whan ſayde thus ſet great powre auctoryte yf vyle valure ſaye yf croked nought theyr maners moche hurte hathe done moche hurte haue ſome done allredy cytie chalcedomianes becauſe prynces preſerued doynge hurte morall vertue namely iuſtyce therfore conuenyent yf maye call conuenyent neceſſarye yt noman ſhal prynce gouernour wante morall vertue namely iuſtyce amonge vertues whiche vertue iuſtyce conuenyent hym ſhal gouernoure certayne vertue aſſocyated called epicikeia vertue iudge dyrected equyte mekenes gentylnes extremytie cruelnes ſpecyallye cheyfly thoſe thynges wherin lawe inſuffycyent vnperfyte getteth playne determynacyon wherfore aryſtotle v boke etykes x chapytre ſayth thus ye nature offyce vertue epicikeia eſteme lawers wyll call equite amende lawe parte halfe wherin vnperfyte maketh expreſſe mencyon ſuffycyently touchynge partyculer thynge becauſe ſpeaketh onely generally epicikeia equyte certayne fauourable interpretacyō moderacyon epicikeiais nature lawe ſome caſe whiche lawe comprehendeth vnder generalyte rygoure whiche thynge lawe ſayde ſo moche vnſuffycyent vnperfyte becauſe hathe excepted ſayde caſe rule whiche wolde haue excepted generalyte rule ſome moderacyon elles vtterlye yf conſydered ſuche caſe ſhulde haue ſo fortuned chaunced agayne beſyde aforeſayd thynges requyred req• red price loue warde cōmune weale hym ſhal prynce gouernoure certayne ſynguler loue beneuolence towardes cōmune weale cytezens reaſon loue beneuolence accyons deades prynce gouernoure intented done dylygentlye better cōmune profyte hole multytude togyther alſo pertyculer profyte eche one hym ſelfe ¶ beſyde theſe ſayde habytes dyſpoſycyons call qualytes neceſſarye prynce gouernoure certayne extrynſecall inſtrument wytte certayne nombre men armes whiche maye execute cyuyle ſentences iudgementes vpon rebelles dyſobedyent perſones coactyue powre wherfore aryſtotle vii boke polytykes viii chapytre ſayth thus lyue togyther cyuyle cōmunyte neceſſarye haue arma ſaye multytude men armes compelle thoſe rebellons dyſobedyent perſones obeye heed offycers gouernours elles lawes cyuyle ſentences ſhulde ydle ſerue nought yf execucyon myght done performed armed powre prynce gouernour nede ſo great excede powre one ſubiecte vnder hym great many howe many maner men armes ought aboute prynce cauſe yet ought reaſon ſo great armed powre vyolate breke lawes rule imperyouſlye lordely beſyde contrarye lawes aryſtotle thyrde polytykes xi chapytre ſaythe wyſe kynge gouernoure ought haue ſo great powre may greatter myghte ſtrength eche one cōmunes hym ſelfe many togyther wherfore ſaye ben thre thynges whiche ought haue ſhall take vpon pryncypall moſte hyghe offyces fyrſt loue preſente ſtate cōmune weale ſeconde haue great powre execute thoſe thynges whiche theyr offyce requyreth thyrde haue vertue iuſtyce vertue vnderſtandeth prudence bonde mayſtres teacher vertues wherfore aryſtotle vi boke etykes laſte chapytre ſayth thus whome ſoeuer prudence whiche one vertue hym alſo ſayde prudence vertues aryſtotle ſayd ſentēce dyd ſet prudence moral vertue vnder one ſame parte ſayde deuyſyon becauſe ſeparated dyſſeuered tyme one whiche mynde ſentence ſemeth ſame boke ſame chapytre whan ſaythe thus manyfeſte therfore euydent premyſſes poſſyble man properly pryncypallye good without prudence neyther man prudent without morall vertue aryſtotle v koke polytykes ix chapytre wryteth thynges whiche haue entreated conuenyent neceſſarye hym ſhall prynce gouernoure perauenture contrarye ordre ben neceſſarelye requyred declared premyſſes appereth propre ſubiecte matere materyall cauſe lawes propre ſubiecte mās lawes men truly prynce gouernour ſhal ſuffycyently prepared wiſdome prudence morall vertue namely iuſtyce maner perſone prynce gouernoure ought thynges conuenyent neceſſarye hym let determyned wyſe ¶ yt prynce cōmunyte kyngdome herte ſenſyble creature ye without kynge prynce cōmunytie kyngdome ſtande partly prynces duetye xv chapytre herte ſenſyble creature fyrſt fourmed noble perfyte qualytes dyſpoſycions al partes ſenſyble creature natura generās hath ſet ordayned powre inſtrument reſydue partes ſenſyble creature fourmed cōuenyēt matere ſubſtaūce alſo ſeperated dyſſeuered ordred eche cōparyſon kepte theyr dyſpoſycyons qualytes alſo preſerued noyaunce hurte moch nature doth ſuffre hym preſerued whan fallen theyr owne nature reaſon ſycknes impedyment repayred reſtored theyr owne nature agayne vertue powre parte ¶ proporcyonatly moche lyke vnto theſe thynges muſt cōſydre cyuyle cōmunyte beynge inſtituted cōuenyētly accordynge reaſon ſoule mynde hole multytude cytezens cōmunes el bygger parte therof fourmed ought fourmed cyuyle cōmunyte one parte fyrſt beynge proporcynated lyke vnto herte ſenſyble creature parte ſetteth ordayneth certayne vertue powre certayne fourme actyue powre auctoryte inſtytute partes cyuyle cō munyte parte wherof meane ye prīce hed gouernour whoſe vnyuerſall vertue powre cauſalite lawe whoſe actyue powre auctoryte iudgynge cōmaundynge executynge ſentences cō cernynge cyuyle ryghtes vtylytes wherfore aryſtotle vii boke polytykes viii chapytre ſayd parte moſte neceſſary al partes cyuyle cōmunyte cauſe hereof ſuffycyencie partes offyces cyuyle cōmunyte thoughe ſayde partes offyces myght ſuffycyētly meanes without prynce gouernour realme cōmune weale cannot contynue thynges thoughe ſo eaſely ¶ without prynce gouernour cyuyle cōmunyte contynue longe cōtynue endure neceſſary otherwyſe offencyous euyll occaſyons ſhall chaunce ſayde goſpell matheue whiche offendicles ſcrypture calleth cōtencyons ryſen amōge men iniuryes done one yf ſhuld iudged meaſured rule ryghtfull thynges iuſtyce wyt lawe prynce gouernour whoſe offyce meaſure ſuche thynges accordynge lawe myght chaunce haply prynce ought ſurmount vertue prudence reaſon therof fyghtyng ſeperacyon men beynge congregated cyuyle cōmunyte priuacyon lacke ſuffycient lyfe pyrnce alſo cyuyle cōmunyte ought noble perfyte dyſpoſycions qualytes yt wyt prudēce vertue morall partes cyuyle cōmunyte reaſon cauſe effectyue cyuyle cōmunyte wyt ſoule wyll hole cōmunyte haue gyuen pryncypall fyrſte parte hathe put hym certayne generall vertue powre cauſalyte wytte lawe alſo auctorytye powre worke execucyon ſayd lawes naturall heate herte beynge ſubiecte heate herte fourme therof performeth accyons dyrected meaſured workynge fourme vertue powre herte elles ſhulde worke due ende agayne alſo heate whiche call cōmunelye ſpyryte beynge inſtrumente performe fulfyl accyons operacyons gouerned throughe hole bodye ſame vertue powre elles neyther outher theſe heates ſhulde worke vnto due ende fyre worketh worſe organ inſtrumentes red ſeconde boke de generatione deanima euen ſo lyke maner auctoryte rulynge gouernynge gyuen man whiche haue called ſpyryte ought bothe ruled meaſured lawe gyuynge iudgementes cōmaundynge executynge cyuyle ryghtes vtylytes el prynce gouernoure ſhulde worke due ende wyt conſeruacyon cyuyle hare brayned felowes men ſmal cōſcyēce leſſe deſcrecyon ought inſtytute ordayne dyuerſe ſundrye partes offyces cyuyle cōmunyte conuenyent matere wytte men hauynge artes habytes qualytes conuenyent xiiii chapitre theſe wordes therfore lawe maker gyueth lawe ought haue reſpecte aforeſayde thynges bothe partes cyuyle cōmunytie alſo accyons ſame alſo ſayd viii boke polytykes fyrſt chapytre whan ſayd thus lawe maker neade ought dylygent take great hede touchynge ordrynge dyſcyplyne yonge men man verely wyl doubte yf thynge dylygentlye ſene vnto cyuyle cōmunytes ſhal hurte moch cōmune weale thus theſe premyſſes appereth ye law maker vnyuerſal multitude ye parlyamēt aſſēbled ye prīces cōmaundement ſame purpoſe apperteyneth belongeth determynacyon meaneth ſuche offyces ye prynce kynge belongeth auctoryte gyuynge lawes wherfore lawfull man take vpon hym offyce cyuyle cōmunyte owne pleaſure namely ſtraungers euery man ought neyther reaſonablie maye owne pleaſure tourne hym ſelfe hyſtory prerogatyue whiche dyſcyple apoſtle ſemed haue comparyſon apoſtles keyes fyrſte promyſed hym afore wordes ſcrypture heretofore brought reherſed certayne thynges ſpoken chryſt hym ſyngulerly ſhal reherſed certayne byſſhoppes hym apoſtolyke epyſcopalſee rome namely ſyns tyme conſtantyne emperour rome ſaye chalenge themſelues aboue byſſhoppes worlde touchynge maner auctoryte iuryſdyccyon yea certayne ſame whiche hathe ben latter tyme onely dothe chalenge aboue preeſtes byſſhoppes alſo aboue prynces world al cōmunaltyes al maner perſones albeit expreſſe egally neyther ſaye playnly openly prynce ruler romaynes called emperoure prouynces cyties perſones ſubiectes ſame emperour albeit ſynguler expreſſy ſuche domynyon coactyue iuryſdyccyon ouer prynce accordynge trouth ſemeth haue taken face fyrſte begynnynge certayne gyfte graunt whiche certayne men ſaythe haue ben made conſtantyne donacyon gyfte cōſtantyne emperour ſaynt sylueſter byſſhop rome yet becauſe clerely expreſſed graunte pryuylege elles becauſe perauenture hath ben dyſanulled made afterwardes elles becauſe weake ſmal ſtrē gthe vertue ſayde graunte extendeth itſelfe lordſhyppes gouernaunces world empyre romaynes al puynces therfore afterwardes byſſhoppes rome latter tyme haue chalenged taken themſelues iuryſdyccyon coactyue vnyuerſally vpon ye hole worlde certayne tytle comprehendynge men wyt fulnes powre auctoryte whiche ſay gyuen chryſte ſaynt peter ſucceſſours epyſcopall ſee rome beynge chryſtes vycares debytes chryſte ſaye truly kynge kynges lord lordes yea hole world bothe perſons thynges dothe folowe thynge whiche wolde inferre conclude ſhall appere certaynely vndoubtedlye thoſe thynges ſhall ſpoken meanynge tytle amonge byſſhoppes rome lykewyſe chryſte fulneſſe powre iuryſdyccyon henry vii worſhypfull memorye laſt emperour rome name whyles reuokynge certayne ſentence iudgement ſame henry vttereth certayne order wordes expreſſynge haue ſayd touchynge theyr ſence meanynge aboute foreſayd tytle whiche wordes leaue paſſe ouer partly becauſe mater knowen well ynoughe partly cauſe ſhortnes becauſe ſhall brynge purpoſe xxv chapytre ye ſeconde dyccyon xviii parte ſame chapytre enſuynge manyfeſtly doth teache ſame decretall ſhal brought v xx chapytre ſeconde dyccyon viii parte ſame chapitre decretall defyneth determyneth beleued good artycle fayth worthye ſucha byſſhop abuſe ſubiectes byſſhoppes rome lytle lytle haue caughte vnto ſelues one iuryſdyccyon namely whan imperyall ſee hath ben vacante yet ſe nowe ſaye theyr ſelues haue imperyall iuryſdyccyon coactyue aboue ſame prynce emperour amonge whiche ſayd byſſhoppes rome byſſhop nowe hath wryten moſt large moſt manyfeſtlye emperour romaynes wel prouynces italye germanye al inferyour prynces ruler ſayd prouynces cōmunytes companyes felyſſhyppes ſynguler perſones ſame ſoeuer dygnyte condycyon man make people byleue abhomynable p̄ſumpcyon pryde eſtate hym ſelfe hath hygheſt chefe iuryſdyccyon vpon al theyr temporalles aſcrybynge openly hym ſelfe powre gyue tranſlate theyr kyngdomes offyces men clerely euydently maye appere men certayne wrytynges ſame byſſhop callethe wrytynges decree ſentēces therfore wronge exyſtymacyon opynyon iudgement perauenture peruerſe affeccyon deſyre domynyon chefe rule whiche chalenge due ſelues byſſhoppes rome theyr deſyrynge domynyō hath ben ye cauſers dyſcorde warres tytle ful powre auctoryte gyuen vnto chryſt ſay ſynguler ſpecyall cauſe whiche haue ſayde maker intranquyllytie dyſcorde cytie realme peruerſe affeccyon beynge prone redy crepe realmes kyngdomes ſayd prohemye noyſome hatefull accyon workynge hath longe ſeaſon vexed realme italye hath kepte contynually doth kepe trāquyllyte peace letteth forbyddeth enforcement promocyon inſtytucyon chefe ruler ſaye emperoure romaynes operacyon workynge ſayde empyre lacke wante whiche accyon worke wyt iuſtyfycacyon cyuyle actes dedes wronges contencyons ſtryfes eaſelye lyghtly doth chaunce ryſe whiche wronges meaſured rule iuſtyce lawe becauſe meaſurer abſent cauſeth fyghtynges reaſon wherof ſeperacyons cōmons inconcluſyon breakynges louſynges cōmune weales italye hathe chaunced haue ſayd throughe opynyon perauenture affeccyon deſyre domynyon bearynge chefe rule wherof haue ſpoken byſſhop rome enforceth laboureth make ye emperour romaynes ſubiecte hym coactyue tē porall iuryſdyccyon emperour neyther ought ryght ſhal playnly openly ſhewed thoſe thynges whiche ſhall folowe neyther coactyue iuryſdiccion apperteyneth ſpyrytual mynyſtre church concernynge ſpyrytual myniſtre wyllynge ſubiecte hym ſuche iudgement offyce coactyue iuryſdyccyon greynge conuenyent neyther byſſhop rome neyther byſſhop ſpyrytuall mynyſtre ſpyrytuall mynyſtre neyther conuenyent haue ſuche iuryſdyccyon ouer man perſon ſoeuer eſtate condycyon ouer cō munytye company felowſhyp hath ben determyned xv xvii chapytres fyrſte dyccyon parte mynde aryſtotle iiii polytykes ¶ becauſe pernycyous peſtylence myſchefe vtterly cōtrary quyetnes reſt men alſo al theyr welthe felycytye throughe faulte ſayde corrupte rote ambycyons affeccyon reygne ouer myght infecte poyſone kyngdomes realmes worlde cheyfely chryſtendome thynke moſte neceſſarye nedefull repell dryue backe ſayd prohemye fyrſte openynge couerynge cloſer howe oppreſſe ye vſurped powre man rome aforeſayde opynyon whiche rote cuylles whiche haue ben done alredye el hereafter ſhall done afterwarde kepynge vnder exteryor outwarde laboure dylygēce ygnoraunte vnryghtuouſe bryngers vp deuyſers alſo frowarde defender ſame theſe thynges men bounde whiche outher haue knowlege myght powre withſtande whiche thynge ſoeuer outher dothe regarde leneth vndone iniuſte vnryghtuouſe wytneſſe tully fyrſt boke de officiis v chapytre whan ſayd two kyndes īiuſtyce dothe reſyſte cuyl mē iniuſte ꝑſones vnryghtuouſnes one doth iniurye wronge men whiche dothe withſtande dryue backe iniurye wrōge whome done yf able powre beholde accordynge notable ſentence tully onely vnryghtuouſe perſons whiche dothe iniurye wronge alſo whiche hathe knowlege able forbyd let whiche dothe iniurye dothe prohybyte let euery one v bounden certayne maner lawe naturall yt wyt dutye frendſhyp ſocyete felowſhyp man whiche lawe left ſhulde wyttynglye tranſgreſſe myght leaſte wyſe ſeme ſelfe vniuſt vnryghtuouſe ſuppoſe put dryue awaye peſtylence myſchefe bretherne faythfull people chryſte fyrſte lernynge conſequently myne outwarde laboure dylygence ſuche ſhall able moche gyuen aboue thynke perceyue vndoubtelye knowe ſophyſme ſubtyltye therof powre open vnto whiche ſophyſme deceytefull cautell peruerſe croked opynyon perauenture alſo peruerſe affeccion vnyted thereunto certayne byſſhoppes rome heretofore preſēt tyme alſo beynge theyr cōplyces whiche theyr mother cauſe aforeſayde ſlaunders hurtes haue lyued truſted hetherto contynuallye laboureth ſuſtayned maynteyned holden vp ſame ¶ thus endeth fyrſte boke ¶ ſeconde dyccyon parte marſilius padwaye powre auctoryte emperoure pope ¶ thre impedymentes maners wayes contrarye ſaye agaynſt veryties contayned dyccyon intencyon thynges whiche ſhall treated maner forme procedynge fyrſte chapytre howe therfore beynge aboute take hande ſette vpon ſo harde hyghe thynge albeit doubte thynge obiected agaynſt v whiche maye grounded vpon trouthe yet natwithſtandynge ſe warres bataylles prepared made redy agaynſt worke iii hate fyrſte aduerſarye agaynſt truthe full mortall enemyes truthe one perſecuſyon vyolent ſerce powre byſſhoppes rome theyr complyces ſhall endeuer ſelfe laboure euer maye deſtroye worke publyſſhers declarer tellynge trouthe beynge dyrectlye contrarye theyr purpoſe witholdynge poſſeſſynge wrongfullye temporalles alſo beynge agaynſt feruent deſyre whiche haue haue domynyon bete rule whiche ſayde purpoſe deſyre ſhall harde thynge great mayſterye reuoke call awaye ſpeche truthe neuer ſo manyfeſt playne opyn yet praye charytable deſyre marſilius god mercy wyll grace vouchſafe reuoke abate kepe vnder vyolent powre faythfull people bothe prynces ſubiectes maye tame holde vnder ſame powre tranquyllyte quietnes al whiche prynces ſubiectes fooes enemyes ¶ ſeconde aduerſary leſſe prepareth batayle agaynſt worke ye ſeconde aduerſary truthe cuſtome lye olde enemye maner euery verytye truthe yt wyt cuſtome herynge falſe lye gyuynge credence ſame falſe lye ſaye haue bene longe ſeaſon ſome preeſtes byſſhoppes theyr ſuffraganes ſowne roted ſowles many ſymple chryſten people theſe preeſtes certayne theyr ſpeches alſo wrytynges hathe entangeled wrapped ſentence god man dyuers implycacyon actes dedes men well relygyouſe laye temporall verye laboryouſe explycated declared inſertynge concludynge afterwardes thoughe vnduelye vntruly ſuch wreſtynge wrythynge ſentences certayne ſences meanynges whiche haue brought theyr iniuſte wrongfull domynyon lordſhyp ouer vpon faythfull people chryſte gyuynge credence throughe theyr owne ſymplycyte certayne deceytefull crafty argumentes theſe preeſtes certayne cōmynacyon thretenynge euerlaſtynge dāpnacyon yt boūden ye ordynaūce god ye obſeruacyon ſuch ſophyſtical ſayēges wrytīges often tymes treſpaſſe amyſſe inferrynge concluſyon ſuch thynges wherof doth dewelye folowe true meanynge thynges wherof queſtyon dyſputacyon made theyr true ſymple begynnynges beynge wyped myndes men falſe vnderſtādynges beynge brought lytle lytle theyr myndes ſtede nowe dyſcernynge bothe hyd many men cuſtome herynge falſe vntrue thynges ſoeuer dyſcyplyne troubeleth leadeth men greatlye awaye trouthe aryſtotle wytneſſeth laſt chapytre phyloſophye reaſon whiche ſayd cuſtome reader hearer boke alſo ſhall greatly troubled letted begynnynge cheyfely ſuche ſhall vnſkylled phyloſophye vnexercyſed holye ſcryptures perceruynge vnderſtandynge alſo perfyte beleuynge verytyes boke contayned ¶ thyrde laſt hatefull noyſome enemye trouthe ſhall great thyrde aduerſarye truthe enuye impedyment lettynge doctryne alſo enuye alſo whiche albeit ſhall beleue haue ſayde ſpoken troutheyet natwithſtādynge becauſe ſhall perceyue man haue ben declarer ſetter forthe trewe ſentence afore ſelues beynge mouyd therunto moſte wycked ſpyryte brennynge enuye ſhal ſet ſelues aduerſaryes agaynſt ſame declarer outher tearynge hym ſecrete preuye backebytynge detraccyon elles clamorouſe barkynge preſumpcyon ¶ wyll leue ceaſe purpoſe neyther feare drede vyolente powre preeſtes otherwyſe ought feruently deſyre domynyon lordſhyp whome ſpeake theſe wrytynges moche maker pſalmes ſaythe lorde helper wyl feare man vnto neyther wyll leue obloquyes enuyouſe detractours expreſſe thynge whiche beynge declared opened may moche profyte good men myght hurte men yf neglected regarded taken heade theſe foreſayde enuyoue perſons ſhall alſo theyr enuye freatynge vexynge tourmē tynge theyr myndes moſt harme vnto ſelues enuye ſaythe vgutio enuye well deſcrybynge it▪ thynge retournynge auctoure therof tormentynge mynde conſumynge waſtynge awaye becauſe mannes welthe good cuſtome afore ſayd enemye v ſhall ſuffycyentlye reſyſted euydence verytes whiche hereafter ſhall ſayde ſpoken ¶ ſhall maner proceſſe ſeconde dyccyon parte ordre procedynge dyccyon parte boke fyrſte ſhall brynge auctorytes holy canon certayne fayned ſtraunge vnmete interpretacyons certayne men whiche peraduenture myght ſeme appere myght proued hygheſt iuryſdyccyon coactyue cheyfeſt rule domynyon dewe ryght byſſhop rome namely lawe chryſten men well aboue prynce emperour romaynes vpon al kyngdomes lordſhyppes cōmunyties companyes feloſhyppes ſyngulare perſones euen ſeculers ſo moche ouer preeſtes byſſhoppes deacon collegyes feloſhyppes ſyngulare perſones eſtate ſoeuer yf neceſſyte iuryſdyccyon maye concluded vertue ſtrength wordes ſcrypture ouer one theſe outher ſeculers clarkes ſame maye comparyſon reſydewe conſequentlye theſe auctorytes ſhall brynge certayne polytyke reaſons apparant confyrmacyon fortefyenge ſayde purpoſe grounded vpon certayne verytes holy ſcrypture whiche alſo euery one trewe agreable men wolde perauēture ſuppoſe theſe reaſons ſay wyll bryng intēte yt may ſo openly dyſſolue make anſwere man henſforthe may lyke deceyued begyled ſolucyon infyrmyte weakenes feblenes aforeſayde opynyon may appere ye whiche longe ſeaſon hytherto haue gyuen coloure face probalyte lykelyhod theſe thynges done ſhall contrary parte brynge certayne verytes holy canon expoſycyons holy interpretours therof fayned ſtraūge falſe agreable mete properly belongynge ſame ſayde verytes doth ſhewe openly playnly yt byſſhop rome called pope byſſhop rome hath iuryſdiccyon ouer preeſtes preeſt byſſhop ſpyrytuall mynyſtre ioyntlie ſonderly ſuche mynyſtres neyther hathe neyther ought haue iuryſdyccyon coactyue man reall perſonall ouer preeſt byſſhop deacon college feloſhyp therfore ſo moche ye leſſe cōmunely ſeuerally hathe ſuch maner iuriſdyccyon vpō kīge prīce vpō realme cōmunalte cōpany feloſhyp ſyngulare perſone ſeculer except onely yt ſuche maner iuryſdyccyon ſome man maker lawe yt prouynce ſhall graunted ſome preeſt byſſhop ſome college feloſhyp demōſtracyon confyrmacyon wherof may ought brought whan man ſhall ſe oportunyte certayne cyuyle polityke demō ſtracyons reaſons whoſe propre prynciples begynnynges cōteyned y• xii chapytre fyrſt dyccyon xv xvii dyſpoſed reherſe agayne becauſe ſhortenynge ſpeche cōſequently aft theſe thyngꝭ ſhall ſhewe howe great powre auctoryte preeſthod keyes gyuen chryſt byſſhop rome euery preeſt manyfeſtacyon declaracyon theſe thynges hāgeth ſolucyon many doubtes whiche ſolucyon gyueth entraunce cōmynge verytie ende ſeche labour brynge forthe afterwardes ſhall profytable ſay ſomwhat make anſwere certayne queſtyons ryſynge aforeſayde thynges whiche ſhall alſo ſaye ſomwhat pryuyleges emperours rome whiche hathe ben graunted ſayd byſſhoppes rome whiche thynge ſhall expedyent profytable buſynes purpoſed entended theſe pryuylegyes vſurpacyons occupacyons withholdynges iuryſdyccyons coactyue nowe aſcrybe properly auctorytie byſſhop rome accaſyonally toke theyr begynnīge cuſtomeor rather abuſe afterwardes hathe taken ſtrength namely emperyall ſeate beynge vacāte theſe pryuylegyes begynnynge nothynge el byſſhopes rome hath ben vpholden purchaſynge gettynge coactyue note iuryſdyccyons cōſeruacyon kepynge ſame afterwardꝭ outher becauſe throughe theyr demerytes haue ben depryued ſame pryuylegies elles left debylytye weakenes occaſyons trouthe iuryſdyccyon vndewely wrongfully taken vnto myght appere couer hyde theyr vnkyndnes el perauenture ſhewed lyke true laſt chapytre fyrſt dyccyon becauſe intende purpoſe occupacyon y• coactyue iuryſdyccyon realmes afore reherſed pryuylegyes coulde nothynge helpe make therfore vſe ſame pryuylegies vnyuerſall tytle afore reherſed make prynces ruler men yt lyueth cyuyllye ſubiectes ſelues wyt fulneſſe powre auctoryte fulnes powre gyuen ſay chryſte ſaynt peter vycate debyte nowe euery byſſhop rome ſucceſſoure peter ſaythe ſelfe hathe hygheſt coactyue iuryſdyccyon al men prouynces reſydewe remenaūte dyccyon ſhall ſhewe auctorytes ye holy canon agaynſt ſentence trouth ſcrypture haue ſayd dothe nothynge make aforeſayd errour rather dothe make agaynſt ſame ſhall manyfeſtly appere expoſycyons certayne ſayntes alſo approued doctours chryſten faythe whiche alſo ſhall playnly appere expoſycyons nay rather ſpeke trulye fyccyons fayned ymagymacyons certayne men goynge aboute wrethe wreſte ſcrypture mayntenaunce fortefyenge ſence theyr falſe opynyon aforeſayd vyolent xxii chapytre luke body whiche gyuen ſaythe gloſe betokeneth body chryſte gyuen whome chryſte ſuffered paſſyon blode ſhed ye apoſtles onely ye whole nature man ſake ſo ye blode chryſte ſhed onelie theſe auctoryties let v fyrſt put ordre wordes whiche xvi chapytre mathewe chryſte ſpeakynge peter ſaythe wyll gyue keyes kyngdome heuen ſoeuer thynge thou ſhalte bynde vpon erthe ſhal alſo boūden heuen ſoeuer thynge thou ſhalt louſe vpon ye earthe ſhal alſo louſed heuens thoſe wordes certayne byſſhoppes wherof ye pope hath taken hymſelfe auctoryte reygne rule rome haue chalenged taken ſelues cheyfly vnder domynyon byſſhop rome hygheſt ſuche iudges ruler ¶ agayne argue euen ſame grounde lykewyſe bodelye ſeconde thynges ben comparyſon ſpyrytuall thynges euen ſo heed bodelye thynges ferre vnder ſubiecte hym whiche ruler ſpyrytuall thynges ¶ moreouer loke comparyſon betwene one fynall ende betwene thyrde lawe betwene maker one law maker lawe euen lyke comparyſon dyfference betwene hym gouerneth accordynge one hym gouerneth accordynge fynall ende whereunto eccleſiaſticall iudge dyrecteth guydeth outher preeſt byſſhop lawe accordynge whiche dyrecteth maker alſo lawe ſuperyours bothe god man myght haue gyuen onely apoſtles alſo maner men auctoryte iuryſdyccyon coactyue worlde aboue prynces ruler domynyons ſynguler perſones greatter powre perauenture make creature dyſtroye kīgdome gouernaunce beynge gouernours coactyue iuryſdyccyon gouernaunce maner coactyue iudgement worlde chryſte wylled exclude dyd exclude hym ſelfe apoſtles bothe touchynge purpoſe intencyon alſo doctryne operacyon workynge appereth vndoubted lye fyrſte ordre wordes texte goſpell iohn̄ xviii chapytre whan chryſte accuſed ponce pylate emperoures vycare deputie iurye ſayd hym ſelfe kynge iewes pylate dyd axe chryſte whether ſayde theſe wordes whether dyd ſaye hym ſelfe kynge chryſte amonge thynges anſwered theſe wordes pylates queſtyon demaunde kyngdome worlde iohn̄ xviii ſaye cōmen reygne temporall gouernaunce domynyon whiche maner kyngꝭ worlde reygne probacyon wherof chryſte hym ſelfe putteth afterward euydent ſygne token whan ſayd yf kyngdome worlde mynyſtres ſeruauntes doubtles wolde ſtryue ſhulde delyuered iewes yf chryſte made argument reaſon yf came worlde haue raygned worldely coactyue gouernaunce rule without doubte ſhulde haue mynyſtres ſame gouernaunce ſhulde fyghte punyſſhe trāſgreſſours lykewyſe kynges haue haue ſuche maner mynyſtres thou thy ſelfe mayſt manyfeſtlye ſe wherof gloſe interlyneare ſayth appereth man deſendeth chryſte reherſynge agayne kyngdō chryſte ſayth nowe kyngdome worlde wyt kyngdome wherof come teache verytyes trewe textes goſpel ſayntes doctours expownynge ſaye thus fyrſte blyſſed auguſtyne theſe wordes ſayenge yf whan pylate aſked demaunded made anſwere forthwith myght haue ſemed haue anſwered alſo iewes onely gentyles hauynge opynyon hym anſwere pylate conuenyentlye metelye anſwered iewes gentyles yf ſayde herken iewes gentyles lette domynacyon rulynge worlde wolde haue come nowe faythe beleue kyngdome whiche worlde nowe chryſtes kyngdome thoſe beleueth hym beholde kyngdome came teache dyſpoſe verely actes workes men dothe come euerlaſtynge kyngdome wytte werkes faythe theologyall vertues yet notwithſtandynge cōpellynge conſtraynynge man kyngdome faythe ſhall playnelye appere hereafter two coactyue domynyons reſpecte one multytude beynge one power ſubiecte letteth ſelues ſhewed viii chapytre fyrſte dyccyon chryſte came let domynyon theſe men ſaynt auguſtyne ſayd wherfore vpon ſayenge ſame chapitre iohn̄ thyne owne people nacyon thyne owne byſſhoppes haue delyuered thynge haſte thou done ſheweth ſuffycyentlye ſayth ſaynt auguſtyne chalengynge worldly domynyon haue ben layde chryſtes charge cryme yf ſhulde ſaye yf thou denyeſt thy ſelfe kynge thynge haſt thou done thou ſhuldeſt delyuered thoughe wold ſaye meruayle ſhulde man delyuered iudge punyſſhed whiche dyd ſaye hym ſelfe kynge beholde accordynge mynde ſaynt auguſtyne chryſte ſhulde haue ben doubtles worthy punyſſhed yf ſayde hym ſelfe haue ben ſeculer kynge namely knowe hym god denyed hym ſelfe kyng kyngdome gouernaunce meaned wytte gouernaunce coactyue tranſgreſſours lawe worlde appereth ſame chapytre iohn̄ vpon texte ſpeakeſt thou thy ſelfe elles hathe men tolde whiche wordes ſaythe theopompus chryſt pylate one moche vnderſtandynge yf ſayde hym pylate yf thou ſpeakeſt thyne owne mynde ſhewe forth token rebellyon yf thou haſt herde reporte men make ordynarye dewe inquyſycyon chryſte ought haue ſayd theopompus ſaythe wyt pylate ſhulde make ordynarie inquyſycyon hym rather ought haue ſayde inquyſycyon dyd appertayne belonge hym becauſe chryſte accordynge opynyon aduerſaryes ryght ſubiecte neyther wolde ſubiecte pylate iuryſdyccyon iudgement coactyue agayne vpon texte kyngdome worlde ſaythe chryſoſtome dothe depryue bereaue worlde prouydence prelacyon preemyttence ſheweth kyngdome worldly tranſytorye corruptyble euery one kyngdomes coactyue worlde humayne tranſytorye corruptyble moreouer vpon texte iohn̄ ſame chapytre thou ſayfte kynge ſaynt auguſtyne ſayth chryſt dyd ſo anſwere feare drede confeſſe knowlege graunte hym ſelfe kynge ſo tēpered anſwere yt neyther dyd denye hym ſelfe kynge neyther yet dyd graunte hym ſelfe ſuche kynge whoſe kyngdome myght ſuppoſed worlde theſe wordes thou ſayfte ſpoken yf ſayde thou carnall man ſpeakeſt carnallye carnall gouernaunce actes temporall cōtentyouſe carnall accordynge thyrde ſygnyfycacyon nowne temporall ſuche actes apoſtle called carnall purpoſe gloſes holy men whiche aduerſaryes knowynge haue ſayd make ryght manyfeſtlye agaynſt euery dyd tourne ſelues allegorycall myſtycall ſence yet notwithſtandynge haue broughte thoſe gloſes alſo greatter confyrmacyon fortefyenge purpoſe leſte myght ſayde aduerſaryes expounde ſcrypture folyſſhelye preſumptuouſlye owne brayne thus ſaythe ſaynt ambroſe expoūdynge theſe wordꝭ chryſte therfore ſubſtaunce xxii mathewe redde whan iewes aſked hym ſayenge tell v howe thynkeſt thou lawful gyue trybute ceſar chryſt loked money quoyne ſcrypture therof made anſwere ſayd gyue ceſar thoſe thynges whiche belongeth ceſar god thoſe thynges whiche appertayneth god gloſe interlyneare ſayth wytte trybute money ſaynt ambroſe vpon texte whoſe ymage superſcrypcyon ſayth wyſe ceſar exacteth requyreth money hauynge ymage imprynted ſo god alſo requyreth ſoule marked lyghte owne face take hede thynge chryſte came exacte worlde chryſoſtome ſayth thus thou thou heareſt theſe wordes gyue ceſar thoſe thynges whiche belongeth hym knowe thou chryſte meaneth onelye thoſe thynges whiche note poynte contrarye vertue cōmaundement god yf ſuche thynge trybute ceſar trybute deuyll beholde thynges oughte ſubiectes ceſar ſo contrarye pytye wytte worſhyppynge god cōmaundement chryſte wolde ſubiecte ſeculer prynces reall temporall ſubſtaunce alſo openlye ſentence mynde ſaynt ambroſe grounded vpon ſentence chryſte ſayde epyſtle agaynſt valentynyan whiche intytled people paye ceſar thoſe thynges whiche belongeth ceſar thoſe thynges belongeth god paye god trybute belongeth ceſar denyed hym ſame thynge ſhewed agayne xvii chapytre mathewe wryten whiche receyued dydrachme came peter ſayde dothe mayſter paye dydrachme conſequentlye certayne wordes betwene foloweth chryſte ſayde peter offende go ſee throwe thyne hoke fyſſhe whiche ſhall come vp fyrſte take vp whan thou haſte opened mouth thou ſhalte fynde ſtotere doble dydrachme take gyue lorde ſayde onelye gyue ſayde gyue ſaynt iherome iherome ſaythe lorde bothe conſernynge bodye alſo ſpyryte ſone worldlye lyuynge kynge two maner wayes fyrſte gendred ſtocke dauid worde ſone almyghtye father therfore oughte ryght trybute paye fre coactyue power bondage beynge ſone kynges afterwarde foloweth ſame ſayenge ſaynt iherome therfore althoughe free yet becauſe taken vpon hym humylytye mekeneſſe nature man ought fulfyll iuſtyce orygen vpon ſayenge chryſte ſaythe maner wyſe offēde ſpeketh wyſe purpoſe mynde euangelyſte whiche maner ſaythe foloweth conſequentlye maye well perceyue ſaythe origen vnderſtande theſe wordes chryſte ofte orygen certayne men ryſeth vp wrongfully taketh away earthly thyngꝭ temporal ſubſtaūce kynges gouernours earthe doth ſende requyre v whiche belongeth owne example lorde forbyddeth occaſyon ſynnynge greyfe gyuen euen ſuche maner men outher leſte myght ſynne elles maye ſaued ſone god whiche neuer dyd ſeruyle worke dede hauynge ye forme ſhape bonde man ſeruaunt toke vpon hym mannes ſake gaue trybute payde money whiche waye byſſhoppes preeſtes exempte vertue ſtrengthe wordes euangelycall ſcrypture yet otherwyſe iuryſdyccion prynces gracyous fauerable graunte ſeynge chryſte peter gyuynge example dyd paye trybute thoughe chryſte whiche bodelye generacyon cōmen ſtocke kynges perauenture dyd owe dutye pay yet peter beynge cōmen ſtocke kynges neyther ſuch cauſe exēpcion neyther yet wyllynge haue yf chryſt thought conuenyent thoughe thoſe whiche ſhulde ſucceſſours hym offyce preeſthode ſhulde paye trybutes theyr temporalles ſhuld vnderneth ye powre prynces gouernours world myght without gyuynge euyll example wyt makynge preeſthode ſubiecte iuryſdyccyon worldly prynces haue ordred dyſpached ryd thoſe exactours gatherer dydrachyn wyt remouynge puttynge away intencyon purpoſe aſkynge ſuche thynges elles ſome cōuenyent way meane chryſte dyd repute thynke conuenyent ſo rather wyllynge paye aſſocyatynge ioynynge hym peter ſyngulerly amonge ye apoſtles notwithſtandynge peter ſhall ſhewe xvi chapitre dyccyon ſhulde afterwarde cheyfeſt doctoure hearde churche ſuche example man ſhulde refuſe ſame saynt ambroſe vnderſtandynge texte ſcrypture taken xvii chapytre mathewe ſuch wyſe haue ſayd epyſtle whoſe tytle ye delyuerīge church ſayth emperour aſketh trybute truly ambroſe denyed hym landes ye churche payeth trybute certayn wordꝭ beynge put betwene ſaythe purpoſe pay ceſar thoſe thyngꝭ whiche belongeth ceſar god thoſe thynges belongeth god trybute belongeth ceſar denyed hym ſaynt bernarde alſo playnly expreſſynge meanynge ye afore reherſed ſcrypture certayne bernarde epyſtle archebyſſhop senon ſaythe wyſe thus ſaye whiche counſayle theyr ſubiectes rebelle agaynſt theyr ſuperyour chryſte ſayth barnarde bothe cōmaunded dyd hym ſelfe otherwyſe gyue ſayth ceſar ſuch thynges apperteyneth vnto ceſar god ſuche thynges payenge trybute belongeth god ſpake mouthe anone gaue hede performe fulfyl worke dede creature maker ceſar greued neyther dyd put paye trybute gaue example ſhulde lykewyſe whan wolde haue denyed dewe reuerence preeſtꝭ god gaue dylygence reuerence euen heathen power offycers worlde ought marke take good hede bernarde ſayth chryſte cared gyue trybute ſeculer power dyd gyue alſo dewe reuerence reuerence coacte compulſyon euery man oweth duetye ſoeuer pay ſuch maner taxe trybute prynces ſhall ſhewe ye chapytre nexte folowenge auctorytie apoſtles xiii chapytre romaynes gloſes ſayntes doctours ſame place moreouer chryſte ſhewed onely hym ſelfe vnder coactyue iuryſdyccyon ye ſeculer price touchyng reall tēporall ſubſtaūce alſo ſheweth ye ſame hym ſelfe touchynge ꝑſon bodye ye perſonal iuryſdyccion poſſyble prynce haue greatter iuryſdyccyon outher vpon hym man whiche cauſe iuryſdyccyon called alſo lawe romaynes mere empyre maye ſhewed euydently xxvii chapytre mathewe red appereth chryſte ſuffered hym ſelfe taken led houſe pylate whiche deputie emperoure rome hym iudge coactyue powre auctorytie ſuffered hym ſelfe iudged delyuered extreme punyſſhement dethe neyther dyd crye agaynſt pylate agaynſt one oughte iudge albeit perauenture gaue knowlege ſuffered ryght wyſe iudgement vndoubtedlye knowen myght haue ſuffered ſuche iudgement punyſſhement preeſtes yf wolde yf iudged inconuenyent ſucceſſours tyme afterwarde come ſhulde ſubiectes ſeculer prynces iudged becauſe ſentence ſeryouſly erneſtly wrytten xix iohn̄ wyll alſo brynge whiche ſayde place whan chryſte brought pylate emperours deputie alſo accuſed ſayde hym ſelfe kynge iewes ſone god whan pylate aſked ieſu whēſe art thou ieſus gyuen therto none anſwere pylate ſayde hym theſe wordes folowynge appertayneth purpoſe wylt thou ſpeake knoweſt thou haue powre auctorytie crucyfie let go lybertie ieſus anſwered thou ſhuldeſt haue powre agaynſt yf gyuen aboue beholde ieſus dyd denye pylate auctorytie iudge hym execute iudgement vpon hym neyther ſayde ryght belongeth dede thus thou doſte chryſte added alſo pylate auctorytye aboue howe aboue auguſtyne maketh anſwere ſayenge let v auguſtyne learne whiche chryſte ſayde whiche taughte apoſtle wyt paule xiii romayns dyd chryſte ſaye taught apoſtle powre ſaye auctorytie iuryſdyccyon god howe ſoeuer acte myſſe vſe powre ſemeth throughe enuye delyuereth innocent powre offycer ſlayne dothe powre offycer ſelfe yf dothe kyll ſlee hym feare dreade hygher greatter powre ſuch powre god gyuen pylate alſo vnder powre ceſar iudyciall coactyue powre pylate ouer perſon chryſt god chryſte ſelfe onely opēly cōfeſſed ſaynt auguſtyne playnly expreſſed ſaynt bernarde ſayde openlye archebyſſhop senon bernarde certayne epyſtle ſayenge chryſte graunteth powre pylate euen ouer hym ſelfe alſo ordayned god theſe bernardes wordes ſpeakynge powre pylate vpon place ſcrypture yf iudiciarie coactyue powre pylate ouer vpon chryſte ſelfe god howe moche vpon tēporall carnal goodes yf chryſt poſſeſſed yf ouer perſone chryſte temporall goodes hadde ſuche auctorytie howe moche ouer vpon perſonages tēporall goodes y• apoſtles theyr ſucceſſours al byſſhops preeſtꝭ thynge onely ſhewed wordes chryſte alſo confyrmed performynge fulfyllynge worke ſame pylate ſyttynge place iudgement ſentence dethe gyuen agaynſt chryſte auctorytie cōmaundement hym execucyon done ſame ſentence theſe wordes ordre red ſame chapytre iohn̄ whan pylate herde theſe wordes brought ieſus forthe ſatte hym ſelfe place iudgemente lytle ſpace foloweth therfore delyuered ieſu vnto ſhulde crucyfyed euen ſuche ſentence opynyon mynde apoſtle paule concernynge chryſte whan ſayde thyrde chapytre galathians whan fulnes tyme cōmen god ſente ſone made woman made vnder lawe foloweth conſequently made vnder iudge alſo whome dyd appertayne iudge cōmaunde accordynge lawe whiche iudge byſſhop preeſt chryſte dyd onely wyl exclude ſeculare gouernaunce iudycyall coactyue powre hym ſelfe alſo dyd exclude apoſtles aſwell one ouer amonge ſelfe comparyſon men wherfore texte xx chapytre mathewe xxii luke made contencyon ſhewynge amonge wyt apoſtles whiche ſhulde greatter chryſte ſayd kynges ruler gentyles haue domynyon ouer whiche hathe powre ouer called benefycyall well doer mathewe clauſe red wyſe whiche greatter exercyſe powre vpon ſhall ſo whiche greatter amōge ſtāde yonger forgoer mayſter mynyſtre whether two greatter ſytteth table mynyſtreth ſerueth ſytteth myddes amonge y• mynyſtreth ſoeuer wyll greatter amōge let hym mynyſtre ſoeuer wyll cheyfe amonge ſhall ſeruaunte euen lykewyſe ſone man came ſerued mynyſtre ſerue temporall thynges lorde ruler egall felowe ſpyrytual mynyſterye offyce cheyfeſt ſeruaunt myddes apoſtles wherupon orygen ſaythe knowe prynces gouernours orygen gentyles lordes hathe domynyon ouer ſaye contente onely gouerne theyr ſubiectꝭ alſo laboureth vyolently lordes powre coactyue yf muſt nedes amōge whiche dyſcyples ſhall ſuche thynges carnal thynges put neceſſytie compulcyon ſpyrytuall thynges wyll ſo let men ye churche loue playe ye lordes chryſoſtome alſo whiche ſpyrytuall ſaye prelate theyr auctorytie gouernaunce ought ſtande loue feare chryſoſtome amonge thynges ſaythe theſe wordꝭ makynge purpoſe prynces world made therfore ſhulde lordes haue domynyon ouer theyr inferyours caſte vnderſeruytude bondage ſpoyle vnderſtande thou yf theyr treſpaſſes euyll deades ſhal deſerue vſe euen deathe theyr owne profyte glorye ruler gouernours churche wyt prelate made therfore ſhulde ſerue theyr inferyours mynyſtre ſoeuer thynges haue receyuyd chryſte ſhulde dyſpyſe theyr owne profyte procure profyte ſhulde refuſe dye helthe ſaluacyon theyr inferyours ſubiectes therfore deſyre prymacye ſoueraygnetye churche neyther ryght neyther profytable wyſe man wyll accorde wyllyngly bynde hym ſelfe ſuche ſeruytude ſuche ieopardie gyue accompte hole churche excepte perauentare ſuch one whiche dredeth iudgement god abuſynge eccleſyaſticall prymacye eccleſiaſtical ꝑſons ought ſeruauntꝭ lordꝭ ruler iherome ſeculer worldely faſcyon ſo dothe tourne ſeculer ſoueraynetie hath preeſtes medlynge ſeculer coactyue iudgementes ought lordes temporally ſeruauntꝭ mynyſtre example precepte chryſte wherfore ſaynt ierome ſaythe fynally chryſte ſetteth forthe afore dyſcyples example owne ſelfe yf apoſtles wolde lytle ſette regarde wordes ſayenges yet leaſte wyſe ſyght workes dedes ſhulde aſhamed lordes vſe domynyon temporally wherfore orygen vpon texte orygen gyue lyfe redempcyon many c ſayth wyſe therfore ruler gouernours churche ought folowe chryſte proude daungerouſe cōmed vnto redy ſoeuer wold come vnto hym ſpake woman layde handes vpon chyldren waſſhed fete dyſcyples yt theyr ſelues may lykewyſe theyr bretherne ſuche maner men ſaythe meanynge prelate tyme ſeme excede paſſe euen worldely prynces pryde outher becauſe vnderſtande perceyue cōmaundement chryſte elles becauſe dyſpyſe ſette nought ſame cōmaundement yf kynges deſyre ſeche armed hoſtes go v thoſe terryble dredefull aſmoche theſe thynges deſpyſe elles ygnoraunte cōmaundement chryſte fyrſte prelate monyſſhed warned hereof whiche thynge ſhall treatyſe ſhewynge declarynge auctorytie conuenyent accordynge mete done yf ſhall regarde amende ſelues ought conſtrayned compelled therunto ſeculer laye prynces leaſt myght corrupte infecte maners men theſe thyngꝭ hytherto reherſed hath ben ſayd vpon mathewe vpon luke baſilius ſayth baſilius magnus wyſe beſemeth ſpyrytuall ruler gouernours offre alſo bodely obſequye ſeruyce example chryſte lorde whiche waſſhed fete dyſcyples therfore chryſte ſayde prynces gentyles lordes ouer wytte apoſtles ſhall ſo chryſte kynge kynges lorde lordes dyd gyue powre auctoryte exercyſe ſeculare iudgementes prynces neyther coactyue powre iuryſdyccyon ouer man openly euydently forbad whan ſayde ſo ſame conſequently holden ſucceſſours apoſtles byſſhoppes preeſtes alſo whiche ſaynt bernarde ſayde openly eugenius ſeconde boke conſyderacyon fourth chapytre treatynge vpon thoſe wordes chryſt afore reherſed kynge prynces gentyles c amonge theſe wordes bernarde whiche apoſtle petre ſame gaue bernard wytte buſy care dylygent ouerſeynge congregacyons dyd gyue domynacyon lordſhyp harken ſaythe hauynge ſaythe domynyon lordeſhyp ouer clargye beynge made example flocke leaſt thou myght wene ſuppoſe ſpoken onely humylytie lowlynes exequyted truthe ſaynge lorde goſpell kynges prynces gentyles haue domynyon lordſhyp ouer whiche haue powre ouer called welldoers benefycyall inferreth concludeth ſo playne y• domynyon forbydden apoſtles ſo may lordes dareſt thou outher beynge lord vſurpe y• offyce apoſtledor beynge apoſtolyke perſone vſurpe domynion lordſhyps forſoth thou art playnly phybyted bothe yf thou art wyllynge haue bothe togyther thou ſhalte loſe elles thynke thy ſelfe excepted nōbre whome god cōplayned wyſe haue reygned haue ben prynces ruler knewe thus veryties treue textes goſpell whiche haue brought alleged interpretacyōs declaracyōs ſame textes made ſayntes approued doctours ought appere euydentlye men chryſte dyd exclude wyllynge exclude hym ſelfe aſwell deades wordes ſoueraynte gouernaunce iudgement coactyue worldely powre auctorytie wolde hym ſelfe ſubiecte vnderneth coactyue iuryſdyccyon ſeculare gouernours prynces hyghe power ¶ canonycall oracle textes apoſtles expoſycyons ſayntes holy doctours whiche ſame thynge openly proued whiche proued chapytre laſte afore gone v chapytre howe reſteth remayneth behynde ſhewe ſame alſo ſentence doctryne cheyfe apoſtles chryſt fyrſt paule whiche ſeconde chapytre ſeconde epyſtle tymothe admonyſſheth aduertyſeth ſame timothe whome ordayned made byſſhop preeſte ſhulde wrappe hym ſelfe worldly buſynes theſe wordes let man warreth god entangle hym ſelfe worldly buſynes gloſe ambroſe mynde ſaythe man warreth god ſpyrytuall thynges whiche god parted deuyded two contrarye ſeruauntes ambroſe euen lykewyſe man ſeruyce two mayſters lordes entangeleth hym ſelfe maner worldly buſyneſſes ſayth maner buſyneſſes exceptynge none aſmoche domynyon iudgement coactyue contentiouſe debatefull actes deades moſt ſeculer worldly buſynes dothe ordre rule ſeculer buſynes ſeculer cyuyle actes men hathe ben ſhewed xv chapytre fyrſt dyccyon apoſtle cōmaundeth pryncypally moſte eſchewed hym ought ſouldyour ſeruaūte god mynyſtringe ſpyrytuall thynges ſo euery maner byſſhop preeſte ought whiche haue reherſed meanynge mynde apoſtle openly euydently declared texte whiche red ſyxte chapytre fyrſte epyſtle corynthyans ſayde wyſe therfore yf haue ſeculer iudgementes ordayne make iudges texte euē nakedly alleged ye authour whiche contemptyble leaſt reputacyon churche apoſtle ſpeake vnto faythfull chryſten men churche moſte propre laſte ſygnyfycacyon whiche ſayde texte apoſtle gloſe expoundeth thus accordynge mynde ambroſe auguſtyne contemptyble ambroſe auguſtyne perſones wyt ſome wyſe men yet whiche leſſe meryte preeſtes teacher goſpell ordayne iudges cauſe ſhewed mynyſtres goſpell ſhulde made iudges ſuche matyers apoſtles goynge aboute place place layſure ſpace gyue theyr mynde ſuche buſynes wyll wyſe holy chryſten men whiche reſtyd abydynge place aboute hyther thyther place place ſprede abrode goſpel ſhulde examyners iudges ſuche buſyneſſe cauſe hereof gloſe aſſygneth accordynge mynde gregory moralles well iudgement accordynge mynde intencyon apoſtle ſayth gregory ought contemptyble perſones byſſhoppes gregorius preeſtes ordayned ſet exercyſe ſeculer offyces doubtles ende ſuche ſhulde examyne earthly worldly cauſes whiche haue gotten wyſdom knowlege exteryor outwarde thynges wyt ſeculer cyuyle actes workes enryched ſpyrytuall gyftes ought entangled encombred earthly matyers buſynes whyles compelled dyſpoſe ordre inferyoure goodes worlde maye able ſeruyce ſuperyour ſpyrytuall good thynges lo moſte euydently mynde apoſtle holy expoſytours haue ſayde offyce vtterly forbydden preeſtes apoſtle paule whiche thynge alſo ſaynt bernarde expreſſynge bernardus eugenius v chapytre fyrſte boke de conſideratione ſayth wyſe dyrectynge ſpeche byſſhops rome place therfore powre auctorytie ſayth crymes ſynnes poſſeſſyons ſynnes poſſeſſyons keyes kyngdome heuens gyuen myght exclude tranſgreſſours ſynners poſſeſſours maye knowe ſayth ſone man hath powre anctorytie forgyue ſynnes afterwardes ſayth whether theſe two ſemeth greatter dygnytie powre forgyue ſynnes elles deuyde parte landes lordſhyppes theſe inferyour vyle earthly thynges haue theyr iudges kynges prynces earthe inuade bondes men vſurpynge belongeth thus foloweth belongeth offyce byſſhoppe preeſtes iudge coactyue iugement contencyous carnall actes temporall thynges rather byſſhoppes preeſtes medlynge ſuche buſynes inuade men boundes ſaye trouble offyce man ſtretch forthe theyr ſythe mannes corne mynde bernarde therfore apoſtle wolde ſhulde iudge coactyue iudgement whiche ordayned mynyſtres goſpell whiche haue goten knowlege exteryoure outwarde thynges wyt cyuyle actes deades moche man treſpaſeth exempte ſuche maner iudgement appereth aſwell preeſtes thoſe ben preeſtes ſubiecte vnderneth coactyue iudgement prynces lay gouernours dylygently marked taken hede apoſtle wrytynge generally chryſten men corynthe appereth ſalutacyon alſo putteth contēptyble perſons churche wyt ſeculer perſons mynde gloſe dothe ſaye ſelfe ordayne ſet contemptyble perſons neyther yet ſuche man iudgeth ſeculer worldly matyers whiche ſhal haue auctorytie neyther lefte behynde hym man ſtede iudge matyers cōſtytute ordayne ſuche maner iudges whiche thynge wolde haue done oughte haue done yf thyng appertaynynge offyce auctoryte aſwel dyd preeſtes byſſhoppes dyd inſtytute ordayne place chryſten congregacyons cōmaunded elles cōmytted make inſtytucyon byſſhoppes preeſtes euydent thyrde chapytre fyrſt epyſtle tymothe fyrſte chapytre ye epyſtle titꝰ thus ſayd titus cauſe haue lefte y• crete lande yt thou ſhuldeſt correcte thoſe thyngꝭ lackynge wantynge yt wytte offence ſynnes treſpaſe yt thou ſhuldeſt put yt whiche good gloſe ſaythe thou ſhuldeſt conſtytute dayne ſet preeſtes euery cytie neyther dyd cōmaunde ſeculet actes iudged byſſhoppes preeſtes dyd rather forbyd wherfore bernarde bernardus place afore alleged ſayth wyſe yet apoſtle iudgeth thynketh ſuch maner ꝑſons ſo moch ſayth neuer one wyſe man amonge whiche maye iudge betwene brother brother ſpeake make abaſſhed aſhamed foloweth ordayne whiche contemptyble perſones churche iudges accordynge mynde apoſtle thou art apoſtolyke perſon doſte vnſembly vnconuenyently vſurpe take vnto thy ſelfe vyle offyce degree contemptyble perſons wherfore apoſtle alſo whiche byſſhoppe ſayd thus inſtructynge byſſhop wyt timothe man warrynge god entangleth hymſelfe ſeculer buſynes ſame bernarde ſayth bernardus afterwarde suppoſeſt thou theſe tymes coulde ſuffre abyde yf men ſtryue go lawe worldlye inherytaunce requyre gyue iudgemente bytwene thou woldeſt make anſwere wordes chryſt men hath ordayned iudge ouer maner iudgement wold men forthwith gyue wolde vplandyſſhe vnlerned man ſay thou knoweſt thy prymacye thou knoweſt bernarde rayleth agaynſt ye ſpyrytualte hyghe magnyfycent ſee thou doſte derogate mynyſſhe apoſtolyke dygnytie yet ſuppoſe wolde ſay thus wyll ſhew tyme apoſtles ſatte iudges ouer men dyuyders termes boundes dyſtrybuters landes ſhorte rede apoſtles ſtode iudged rede yt ſate iudges ſhall ſene perauenture hath ben ſene ſeruaunte iudged mynyſſher dygnyte bycauſe wylleth greatter whiche ſent hym ſame becauſe dothe go beyonde boundes whiche father hath ſette mayſtre lorde hym ſelfe ſayde hathe ordayned made iudge ſhall ſeruaunt thought haue iniurye wronge excepte iudge al men thus bernarde ſayth ſucceſſoure apoſtles dothe vnſemely vnaccordyngly yf vſurpeth taketh vnto hym ſelfe offyce iudge holy apoſtle cōmaunded men indyfferently man excepted neyther byſſhop neyther preeſte deacon oughte vnder iudgemēt coactyue iudges prynces gouernours ſeculer ſuche ſeculer gouernours ought obeyed onleſſe dyd cōmaunde thynge done dyrectlye agaynſt lawe euerlaſtynge ſaluacyon wherfore xiii chapytre romaynes ſaythe let euery ſoule ſubiecte hyghe power powre god thoſe power ordayned god therfore whoſoeuer reſyſteth powre reſyſteth ordynaunce god thoſe whiche reſyſteth dothe purchaſe gette ſelfe dampnacyon prynces gouernours feared well doer dothe euyll wylte thou drede powre good thou ſhalt obtayne prayſe hym mynyſter good yf thou ſhalt euyll feare beareth ſwerde without cauſe mynyſter god punyſſhe vengeaunce hym dothe euyll therfore ſubgiectes ſo ought neceſſytie onely becauſe wrathe alſo becauſe cōſcyence becauſe pay trybutꝭ mynyſters god ſeruynge ſame thyng gyue men theyr dueties trybute trybute due rente rente feare feare honoure honoure due gyuen wyllyng alſo vpon theſe wordes apoſtle worthye noted brynge gloſe mynde ſayntes catholyke doctours becauſe thyſe thynges whiche apoſtle hathe ſayde gloſe maker purpoſe ſo openly euydently ſhewed true man beynge ryght mynde hath ſeen red ought doubte lenger apoſtle ſayd euery ſoule exceptynge none gloſe auguſtynes mynde fyrſte otherwhyles mynde ambroſe ſayth thus prouoketh exhorteth men humblenes certayne men thought euyll lordes ruler namely ſuche infydels ought haue domynyon rule euyll ruler obeyed reuerētly good ruler ouer chryſten men yf good alſo chryſten peetes egall good chryſten men whiche pryde alſo apoſtle putteth awaye euen ſuperyour parte man wytte ſoule betokenynge hole man ſaye euery ſoule euery man yf ſhulde ſaye foreſayde thynges done thoughe ſo perfyte bodye chryſte yet notwithſtandynge let ſoule put ye mā euery ſoule ſubiecte ſaye lette euery man ſubiecte whiche man ſygnyfye therfore name ſoule ſhulde ſerue obeyſſaunte onely bodye alſo wyll mynde therfore let euery ſoule ſo ſubiecte obedyent euen alſo wyll ſerue ſeculer power bothe good euyll wytte kynges prynces gouernours hygh capytaynes vnder capytaynes ſuch lo apoſtle vnderſtode meaned hygher power nothynge elles ſeculer prynces gouernours foloweth gloſe yf good man whiche ruler gouernoure ouer thy nouryſſher yf euyll man temptoure proue aſſaye bothe receyue take nouryſſhementes cheryſſhynges gladlye good wyll thy temptacyon thou approued thou therfore golde marke take hede worlde fornayce golde fyner lette euery ſoule ſubiecte hygher power wyt hyghe worldlye thyngꝭ elles worde hygher ſignyfyed cauſe wherfore ought obeyed becauſe hygher ordenaunce god ¶ power god proueth oughte ſubiectes obeyſſaunte maner waye becauſe power god thoſe thynges whiche god ordeyned god foloweth power auctorytie ordeyned god ſaye ſoeuer hathe power auctorytie hath ordynaunce god therfore ſoeuer reſyſteth power reſyſteth ordynaunce god ſaythe yf oughte therfore ſubiecte becauſe neyther good man neyther euyll hathe power excepte gyuen vnto hym god wherfore oure lorde ſayde pylate thou ſhuldeſt haue power ouer yf gyuen aboue whiche bernardus thyng bernarde alſo repeting archebyſſhop senon ſayth man ſeculare pylate afore lorde ſtode iudged yet ſayde thou ſhuldeſt haue power ouer yf gyuen aboue tyme chryſt ſpake hym ſelfe experyence thynge hym ſelfe whiche thynge cauſed publyſſhed proclaymed throughout church apoſtles wytte power aboue foloweth gloſe thoſe ordeyned god ſaye reſonablye dyſpoſed ordeyned god therfore ſoeuer vyolence dyſcorde gyle reſyſteth power wyt man hauynge power thoſe thynges whiche belonge power trybute ſuche thynges reſyſteth ordynacyon god ſaye reſyſteth hym hath power ordynacyon god therfore dothe accordynge ordynacyon god good power euydent god hath made hym ruler reaſonably without good cauſe euyll power maye alſo appere made ruler reaſonably whyles good men purged hym euyll men cōdempned hym ſelfe caſte downe hedlonge worſe worſe marke take hede ſomtyme worde power vnderſtande worde power power ſelfe auctorytie whiche gyuen god ſomtyme ſame worde vnderſtande man ſelfe hathe power whiche ii sygnyfycacyons let dylygent reader marke one reſyſteth power reſyſteth ordynacyon god ſo greuous offence ſoeuer reſyſteth power purchaſe gette ſelfes euerlaſtynge marke well counceyll dampnacyon therfore man oughte reſyſte ſubiecte obeyſaunte hym yet yf cōmaunde thynge whiche thou oughte doo lawe god truely thou mayſte execute cōmaundemente fearynge greatter power wytte god marke take hede degree wordly thynges yf emperour rome ſhall bydde cōmaunde thynge ſubiects done albeit cōmaū de contrary proconſull agayne yf proconſul whiche emperours ſubiecte offycer vnder hym byddeth one thynge emperour cōmaundeth thynge doute deſpyſynge proconſuls cōmaū deth ſubiecte ought obey emperour pryncipall capytayne therfore yf emperour cōmaūde one thynge god doth cōmaunde thyng ſubiecte ought obey god emperour yet ſaynt auguſtyne ſayd yf emperour cōmaunde one thynge pope byſſhop cō maūde thyng whiche thyng ought haue ſayd yf pope ben ſuperyour emperour degree iuryſdyccyon yet ſaynt auguſtyne wolde yf emperour hathe cōmaunded thynge due agaynſt lawe euerlaſtynge worke thou well thou haſte cauſe wherfore thou nede feare ordrede thou ſhalt rather haue prayſe ſame power althoughe euyll whyles thou haſte cauſe greatter crowne rewarde yf ryghtwyſe power offycer ſhalte prayſed men ſo ſhalt thou truly haue prayſe hym mynyſter god good ſay doynge good whether good euyll gyuen god thy good profyte wytte deſende thyne manyfeſt euydent open ruler gouernoures ſay becauſe fayth doth ſuffre domynion cōpulſion thyng free neceſſytie ſay therfore becauſe ar helper yf worke v yourioy eternal el ioy amēdemēt ar amēded doth ioy ar glad ſaid well ouer faith auguſtyne maketh mēcyon byſſhop preeſt onely ſeculare prynces wherfore apoſtle wylleth ſayth auguſtyne prayer made kynges thoſe whiche hyghe auctorytie yea althoughe euyll men ſheweth cauſe ſayeng ſpotte alſo loſeth ye dette euerlaſtynge deth hathe howe preeſtꝭ haue powre bynde loſe notgraunted powre preeſtes whome yet hathe gyuen powre bynde loſe ſay powre ſhewe declare men bounde loſe whiche wordes hathe expreſſed ende offyce mynyſterye preeſt requyred penaunce declarynge ſame ſayde wherfore alſo lorde reſtored fyrſte hym ſelfe perſone ful leprye helth afterwardes ſent hym preeſtes whoſe iudgement ſhuld ſhewed declared made clene ſame maner alſo hym ſelfe reyſed lazarus agayne lyfe offered hym dyſcyples loſed albeit yt ſome man loſed afore god yet accōpted taken loſed ye face yt ſay knowlege church ye iudgement declaracyon preeſte loſynge therfore retaynynge ſynnes preeſte newe lawe doth ſo worke iudge ye preeſte oldelawe dyd worke iudge defyled lepry lepry betokeneth ſynne ſentence alſo doth repete reherſe agayne aboute ende ſyxte chapytre confyrmeth auctorytie ſaynt ierome vpon ſayenge chryſte xvi chapytre mathewe ſhall gyue keyes kyngdome heuens ſayde ierome ſayth ierome marke well wyſe preeſtes goſpell hathe ſame auctorytie offyce legale preeſtes vnder lawe olde tyme healynge perſones whiche infected leprye theſe therfore preeſtes goſpell dothe forgyue retayne ſynnes whyles pronounce declare ſhewe theyr ſynnes forgyuen retayned god wherfore boke leuiticus leper cō maunded ſhewe ſelues preeſtes whome preeſtes neyther maketh full leprye neyther yet clene ſame onely dyſcerne iudge declare clene perſones vnclene offyce mynyſterie therfore preeſte requyred penytent aforeſayd cauſe wyt hym maye ſhewed declared face churche whome god hathe eyther forgyuen elles retayned theyr ſynnes another thynge alſo whiche god worketh ſynner without mynyſterye preeſte ſame mayſter ſentēces alſo rycharde iudge wyt chaungynge temporall payne purgatory whiche ſynner geare muſte iudged higher iudges whether purgatory lyfe • ſhuld haue ſuffered ſynnes neuer ſo wel penytent confeſſed ſome ſatyſfaccyon worlde faſtynge prayer almoſe dede ſome lyke dede touchynge poynte preeſte exercyſeth ryght powre vpon ſynner wherfore mayſter xviii diſtynccyon vii chapytre ſayth thus noted marked preeſtes bynde men ſatyſfaccyon penaūce ſhewe ſame men loſed theyr ſynnes penytencyall ſatyſfaccyon enioyned man onely hym whome preeſte doth iudge whome penytencyall ſatyſfaccyon moyued truely penytent vnto enioyneth ſatyſfaccyon iudgeth ſynnes retayned god preeſte alſo chaungeth paynes purgatorye dewe ſynner ſome ſatyſfacciōs world afterwardes reconſyleth ſynners churche wyt cōmunyon felowſhyp chriſten men poynte ſemblably doth exercyſe powre ouer ſynners yf ſo accordynge dyſcrecyon iudgement wherfore mayſter place afore alleged ſayth preeſtes alſo dothe bynde whan enioyne ſatyſfaccyon penaunce whoſe confeſſyons haue harde loſe forgyue parte ſame elles whan admytte receyue purged ſuch ſatyſfaccyon cōmunyon felowſhyp chryſten men ye partetakynge ſacramentes maner preeſtes ſayde forgyue retayne ſynnes wherfore ſaynt auguſtyne ſayde afore whome forgyue ſynnes god doth forgyue c exercyſe worke iuſtyce vpon ſynners whan bynde iuſt dewe punyſſhemēt alſo exercyſe y• worke mercye whan releaſe parte ye ſame el recōſyle ye cōmunyon ꝑtetakynge y• ſacramētꝭ workes theſe ye preeſtꝭ excercyſe vpon ſynners wherof may alſo appere euydētly pope gyueth nomore ſynne preeſte yf preeſte dutie bounde gothe purgatorie thē wherfore ſhuld beleue one byſſhop rome maye releaſe ſynne payne may preeſte euer ¶ thus aforeſayd auctorytes ſayntes mayſter ſentences rychard appereth euydently onely god remytteth forgyueth ſynne dette eternall payne true penytent ſynner without worke preeſte outher goynge elles cōmynge betwene hathe ben ſhewed heretofore wher wyll alſo ſhewe infable ſure demonſtracyon argument accordynge ſcrypture ſayenges ſayntes doctours god onely whiche beignoraunt whoſe ſynnes forgyuen whoſe retayned alone whiche moued ſtyrred peruerſe croked affeccyon whiche iudgeth man wrongfully lyke caſe churche preeſt euer euen byſſhop rome euery one maye otherwhyles erre myſtake elles inclyned moued peruerſe affeccyon el wherfore yf ſynne dette eternal payne dāpnacyon ſhuld forgyuen ye true penytēt hauynge dewe put poſe confeſſed alſo hathe ben confeſſed dede becauſe man rayleth preeſte happely dothe retayne ſynne eyther throughe ignoraunce malyce bothe often tymes faythfull promyſe chryſte goſpell ſhulde peryſſhe ſtrengthe truthe wherby ſayde ſhall gyue good men rewardes eternall ioye euyll wycked men euerlaſtynge paynes fyre hell wherfore chaunceth cōmeth paſſe alſo oftentymes put caſe certayne ſynner confeſſed ſynnes faynedly duelye ought ſuche fayned confeſſyon made hath ignoraunce fauoure preeſte elles receyued abſolucyon benedyccyon put caſe agayne certayne ſynner whiche confeſſed ſynnes ſuffycyently duelye preeſte preeſte ignoraunce malyce el throughe bothe refuſed gyue hym abſolucyon benedyccyon ſynnes former perſone cōfeſſed ſynnes faynedly forgyuen ſynnes latter man beynge truely penytent confeſſed yet retayned holden ſtedfaſtlye vndoubtedlye wherfore chriſoſtome vpon theſe wordes xx chapytre iohn̄ receyue holy ghoſt whoſe ſynnes chryſoſtome ye ſhall forgyue c ſaythe thus neyther preeſte neyther yet aungell archaungell may worke thynge thoſe thynges ar gyuen god yet preeſte gyueth benedyccyon putteth hande ryght malyce man aboute ſacramentes helthe thoſe men ſhulde hurte whiche come faythe ſame ierome alſo lytel ierome recyted vpon ſayenge xvi mathewe ſhall gyue keyes kyngdome heuens ſayth thus certayne men vnderſtandynge place take ſelues ſomwhat pryde pharyſeis ſuppoſe ſelues dampne innocentes aſſoyle loſe wycked perſones whan trouthe afore god ſentence preeſtes requyred god regardeth ye lyfe men iudgement preeſtes ſoughte lyfe ſynners perſones accuſed whiche wordes mayſter ſentences vi chapytre xviii dyſtynccyon putteth notable texte folowynge alſo openly ſhewed god foloweth iudgement churche whiche otherwhyles iudgeth ſurrepcyon ignoraunce churche meaneth preeſtes whiche churche addeth alſo viii chapytre ſame dyccyon whyles put forthe ſaye whiche iudged preeſte without churche ſame within church without church vnderſtande thou dede ſemeth retayned within xviii dyſtynccyon ye viii chapytre ſayth thus hathe ben ſhewed howe maner preeſtꝭ forgyue retayne ſynnes yet god hathe reſerued hym ſelfe certayne ſynguler ſpecyall powre forgyuynge retaynynge ſynnes onely hym ſelfe owne auctorytie loſeth forgyueth dette euerlaſtynge dampnacyon purgeth clenſeth ſoule wardly ſame may ſter ſayth alſo ix laſte chapytre ſame dyccyon therfore vnlykeneſſe elongacyon worthely ſtryken ſentence therof grace god proteccyon defence taken awaye lefte themſelues ſo lybertie fall dethe ſynne vpon alſo deuyll hath powre gyuen hym rage cruelly vexe prayer alſo churche ſuffrages helpes benedyccions good workes ſuppoſed nothynge auaylynge nowe knowe perſone perſones maner powre excōmunycacyon curſynge doth appertayne ought fyrſt attende take hede excōmunycacyon ſynner iudged punyſſement ſtate world come certayne iudgemēt wherof ſhall ſpeake expreſſely playnely ix chapitre dyccyon alſo certayne great payne punyſſhement put hym euen ſtate preſent lyfe defamed openlye banyſſhed company men reaſon wherof alſo berefte ye cyuyle cōmunyon cōmodytie albe inflyccyon fyrſte payne hym whiche vnworthely wrong fully ſtryken ſentence excōmunycacyon doth nothynge hurte ſtate worlde come becauſe god doth alwayes folowe iudgement churche ſay preeſtes whan iudge declare man accurſed wrongfully haue ſhewed ſuffycyentlye heretofore yet ſhulde whiche wrongfully ſtryken ſame ſentence preeſte greatly fore hurte ſtate preſente lyfe dyffamed openly berefte company cytezens cyuyle cōmodytyes therfore ſayd albeit voyce wordꝭ preeſte operacyon mynyſterye requyred promulgacyon publyſſhynge ſuche iudgement yet iudgement coactyue powre gyue cōmaūdement excōmunycatynge aſſoylynge perſone perſones dothe note appertayne alone onely colledge cōpanye ordayne make ſuche iudge whome may lawfull call perſone ſo accuſed gyltie afore hym examyne hym iudge hym condempne aſſoyle perſone whiche ſo openly dyffamed cut awaye companye felowſhyp chryſten men doth appertayne belonge ſuperyoure ſoueraygne ſame cōmunyte el counſayle hym apoynted preeſtꝭ onely iudge dyſcerne ſcrypture crymes takynge worde iudgement fyrſt ſygnyfycacion wherfore man ought cut awaye company chryſten men lefte myght infecte men lykewyſe phyſycion company phyſycions muſt iudge iudgement fyrſt ſygnyfycacion bodely dyſeaſe wherfore man ought ſeperated cōpany men left myghte infecte hath coactyue powre expell dryue perſones ful leprye vnto ye hygher power realme towne cytie euen ſo doth appertayne preeſt alone colledge cōpany onely ordayne y• cōmunytie chryſten men iudgement notwithſtandynge accordynge probacions afore brought yf conuycted wytneſſe cryme alſo ſuche wherfore ought excōmunycate perſone founde gylty ſuche cryme ought pronounſed worthy excōmunycated conſyderacyon thynke haue reherſed moche ſuffycyent v purpoſe concernynge maners auctorytie powre gyuen chryſte preeſtꝭ byſſhoppes may proued holy ſcrypture nowe gatherynge togyther agayne makynge ſūme corollary • thoſe thynges whiche haue ben ſayde v concernynge powre auctorytie keyes whiche gyuen chryſte apoſtles preeſtes ſucceſſours let v ſaye ſynner truely penytent ſay beynge ſorowfull ſynne cōmytted god alone worketh ſome thynges euen thyngꝭ god alone worketh man without mynyſtery preeſte goynge wyt illumynatynge mynde purgacyon clenſynge faulte ſporte ſynne remyſſyon euerlaſtynge dampnacyon ſome thynges therbe whiche god worketh ſame ſynner hym ſelfe alone thyngꝭ done ye preeſte mynyſterye preeſte folowynge ſhewe declare face churche accompted bounde loſed ſynnes world ſo ſhall bounde loſed world yt ſay whoſe ſynnes god hathe retayned el forgyuen agayne thynge god worketh aboute ſynner ye mynyſtery preeſt yt wyt chaungynge agreed yet purgatorye aft lyfe payne
