prohybyted mānes lawe yf done agaynſt man preeſt accyons ſpyrytuall therfore dothe appertayne belonge prynce ſeculer gouernoure punyſſhe preeſt ſuche offence treſpaſſes ſuche maner thynges prohybyted lawe aduoutrye maymynge murther thefte robbery dyffamacyon detraction treaſon fraude gyle hereſye ſuche crymes cōmytted done preeſte carnall temporall dedes offence verye well knowen experyence haue declared heretofore ſeconde chapytre dyccyon auctorytie apoſtle thyrde chapytre fyrſte epyſtle corynthians xv romayns ye alſo iudged ſo moche carnall temporall offencꝭ howe moche preeſt byſſhop cōmyttynge ſynneth greuouſly ſhamefully ought call backe ſuche offence gyuynge occaſyon theym redyneſſe offende treſpaſſe ſame throughe lewde vngracyous example ¶ therfore euery preeſte byſſhoppe vndre ought vndre iuryſdyccyon prynces ſecular gouernours thoſe thynges whiche cōmaunded obſerued lawe man aſwell ſeculare laye men neyther byſſhoppe preeſte exempted coactyue iudgement ſuche prynces neyther maye exempte man owne auctoryte whiche thynge proue addycyon thoſe thynges whiche hath ben ſayd xvii chapytre fyrſte dyccyon deduſynge bryngynge hym whiche doth ſaye contrary ameruaylous great inconuenyent yf byſſhop rome pope rome exempte frō iuryſdyccyon offeculare prynces preeſte ſo exempted ſhulde vndre coactyue ryſdyccyon prynces gouernours hym ſelfe ſuche maner iudge without auctorytye humayne lawe maker myght ſeperate exempte ye ſprytuall mynyſters ye cōmune name call clarkes iuryſdyccyon prynces gouernours make ſubiectes hym ſelfe byſſhoppes rome done nowe dayes folowed neceſſarylye iuryſdyccyon ſeculer gouernours maner vtterly adnulled deſtroyed made ſtrength whiche thynge recounte great inconuenyent intollerable gouernours cōmunyties chryſten relygyon dothe depryue man ryght ſhewed afore auctorytie ambroſe vpon ſayenge paule ſeconde chapytre titus admonyſſhe ſubiectes prynces powres c brought alledged v chapytre dyccyon inconuenyent dothe folowe ſuche exempcyon thus proue founde prohybyted goddes lawe rather graunted alſo lawful ſame hym preeſte byſſhop whiche hath wyfe namely yf haue mo wyues one redde thyrde chapytre fyrſt epyſtle tymothe whiche decreed ordayned mannes lawe conſtytucyon maye ſame auctorytie reuoked adnulled mannes lawe therfore byſſhop rome maketh hym ſelfe lawe maker maye fulnes powre yf man wyll graunte hym haue ſuch ful powre graunte preeſtes deacon ſubdeacons haue wyues maye graunted preeſtꝭ haue wyues onely alſo whiche haue taken foreſayd ordres otherwyſe conſecrated whome call clarkes ſyngle tonſure yea moreouer ſemyngly theſe whiche thynge bonifacius viii ſemeth haue done dede myght increaſe ſeculer powre hym ſelfe many hadde maryed virgyne whiche wyllynge wedde one wyfe aſcrybed company charkes decreed ſhuld aſcrybed ordynacyons conſtytucyons call decretales neyther kepynge within theſe boundes haue exempted cyuyle lawes man duely made certayne laye men whome call italy fratres gaudentes place called begymes haue alſo exempted fratres gaudētes begini bretherne called fratres hoſpitaliorum templariorum brethern hoſpytalles templar many ſuche lyke order lykewyſe whiche called dealto paſſu ſo alſo theyr pleaſure myghte lyke maner lyke reaſon wherfore yf ſuch maner men exempte iuryſdyccyon prynces gouernours accordynge theyr decretales alſo gyueth perſones ſo exempted certayne lybertyes imunytes publyke cyuyle chargꝭ burthaynes ſemeth lykelye greater multytude parte men ſhall declyne company namelye ſeynge take receyue indyfferentlye relygyous men receyue men lerned theyr order learned vnlerned euery man prone redye folowe drawe owne profyte auoyde eſchewe owne dyſprofyte yf greater multytude men ſhall declyne company clarkes ſhall iuryſdyccyon coactyue powre prynces remayne ſtrength weake feble whiche great inconuenyence thynge wherby cōmune wealth cyuyle gouernaunce ſhulde deſtroyed ſoeuer enioyeth cyuyle honour cōmodytyes profytes peace defence cheyfe gouernour ought exempte cyuyle chargꝭ burtheyns cyuyle iuryſdyccyon without determynacyon ſame gouernoure aduoydynge therfore great inconuenyent oughte graunte accordynge vnto trouthe hyghe cheyfe gouernoure hath iuryſdyccyon vpon byſſhoppes preeſtes clarkes leſte myght chaunce good ordre cōmune weale broken pluralytie cheyfe gouernoures beynge one vndre determytted xvii fyrſte dyccyon cheyfe gouernour ought determyne apoynte certayne nombre prouynce vnder gouernaunce lykewyſe dothe perſones parte cōmune weale lefte yf dyd growe vp ouer greate multytude myght able reſyſte coactyue powre gouernours otherwyſe great dyſturbaūce cōmune weale elles theyr pryde ouer great multytude depryue cytie realme cōmunytye profyte auauntage theyr neceſſarye workes occupacyons outwarde actes dedes goynge tournynge profyte dyſprofyte ryght wronge ſondry perſone doer ought ruled meaſured humayne lawe iudge thyrde ſygnyfycacyon whiche coactyue iuryſdyccyon ſeculer laye men alſo charkes oughte ſubiectes alſo iudges accordynge lawes lawyer man whiche called iudges fyrſte ſecōde ſygnyfycacion ye teacher ſame lawes yet lackynge wantynge coactiue powre auctorytie whiche ſorte thynge letteth may many ordred one vnder euen one communytie ¶ relacyon reſpecte mannes dedes workes vnto lawe god iudge worlde wytte chryſte alſo howe ſame dedes ar compared teacher ſame lawe wytte byſſhoppe preeſte worlde ix chapytre accordynge therfore maner alſo certayne iudge hauynge coactyue iuryſdyccyon auctoryte vpon tranſgreſſours lawe god whiche lawe alſo haue ſayde coactyue rule ſome dedes workes men well thoſe whiche called actus īmanentes thoſe whiche called actus tranſeuntes iudge one wytte chryſte none wherfore wryten iiii chapytre iames one lawe maker whiche maye dyſtroye delyuer coactyue one lawe maker chryſte powre iudge exerſyſed vpon man world towchynge dyſtrybucyon payne rewarde tranſgreſſours obſeruers lawe īmedyatly gyuen hym whiche often tymes haue called lawe goſpell chryſte great mercy wolde graunte vnto v ſpace wherin myghte penaunce ſynnes cōmytted agaynſt lawe euen vntyll laſte ende euery mannes lyfe ſhall ſhewed hereafter alſo auctorytes holy ſcrypture alſo ſcrypture goſpell iudge fyrſt ſygnyfycacyon lykewyſe mannes iudge taken preacher lawe wytte preeſt whiche worlde teacher goddes lawe ſuche thynges whiche eyther done eſchewed gettynge eternall lyfe aduoydynge payne eternall yet hauynge coactyue powre worlde cōpell man obſeruynge iudge hath coactyue powre preceptes cōmaundementes ſame lawe ſhuld vayne none effecte compell man vnto obſeruynge hym ſhulde obſerue onely compulſyon ſhulde nothynge auayleable clargy many yere hath done cōpulſyon ſwerde fyre vnto eternall helthe ſhewed euydently auctorytie chryſoſtome alſo apoſtle paule v chapytre dyccyon therfore iudge conuenyentlye lykened phyſycyon leche whiche hathe auctorytie gyuen hym teache cōmaunde prenoſtycate iudge thoſe thynges whiche profytable done lefte vndone optaynynge gettynge bodely helthe aduoydynge death ſyckeneſſe whiche ſhulde chaunce hym whiche cauſe chryſte alſo ſtate ſtate preſente lyfe called hym ſelfe phyſycyon leche prynce iudge therfore ſayd vnto pharyſeys ſpeakyng hym ſelfe brought chapytre afore gone nede leche whiche helthe whiche ſycke dyſeaſed chryſte hath ordayned man ſhulde compelled worlde obſeruacyon lawe made hym therfore hathe ordayned iudge ſpyrytuall hauynge coactyue powre punyſſhe tranſgreſſours lawe worlde wherfore marked taken hede lawe goſpell may two maner wayes compared vnto men vpon whome made chryſte one waye maye compared ſtate ſtate preſente lyfe comparyſon maye rather called ſpeculatyue practyue doctryne elles bothe lawe taken propre laſt ſygnyfycacyon albeit maye called lawe ſygnyfycacyons ſame worde ſeconde thyrde ſygnyfycacyons whiche haue ſpoken x chapytre fyrſte dyccyon cauſe whiche haue ſayde name worde lawe thyrde ſygnyfycacyon belongeth onelye coactyue rule wytte ſuch rule accordynge whiche tranſgreſſoure punyſſhed powre coactyue gyuen hym whiche ought iudge accordynge ſame rule nowe lawe goſpell lawe maker therof cōmaunded man ſhulde compelled ſpyrytuall man worlde obſerue thoſe thynges whiche cōmaunded ſame lawe done lefte vndone worlde therfore beynge compared ſtate man worlde worlde ought called doctryne lawe onely ſuche maner haue ſayde mynde apoſtle thyrde chapytre ſeconde epyſtle tymothe ſcrypture inſpyred god aboue profytable teache argue proue rebuke inſtructe ryghtuouſneſſe neuer ſayde profytable compelle punyſſhe worlde wherfore fyrſte chapytre ſeconde epyſtle corynthyanes apoſtle ſayth becauſe lordes gouernours ouer faythe helper comforter ioye becauſe ſtande faythe ſaynt ambroſe haue ſhewed v chapytre dyccyon greueth reherſe ſame often tymes agayne ſayth theſe wordes leſt corynthyanes myght myſcō tent ambroſe angrye yf apoſtle taken vpon hym lorde ouer becauſe ſayd ſparynge haue come therfore apoſtle ſayth followyngely ſaye theſe aforeſayd wordes ſparynge becauſe fayth ſuffereth domynyon compulſyon fayth voluntarye whiche thynge freewyll neceſſytye ſpeake theſe wordes therfore becauſe helper yf wyll worke v c loo ſayth helper wyt doctryne ſaythe alſo yf wyll worke v whiche nowe ſtande faythe worketh loue domynyon compulcyon maner way ſcryꝑture lawe yf men ſeme punyſſhed breakynge goddes lawe world cōmittīge aduoutry nycaciō theft hereſy ſo forth becauſe malyce theyr hertꝭ breketh forth diſq•eteth theyr neyghbours therby offē deth ye kyngꝭ lawe ī reſpecte offende goddes lawe whiche onely referred god punyſſhed euerlaſtīgly goſpell maye compared vnto men ſtate worlde whiche worlde onely ſhal payned punyſſhed whoſoeuer hath tranſgreſſed broken ſayd lawe worlde ſo maye well called lawe moſte propre ſygnyfycacion iudgeth accordynge whiche chryſte maye called iudge moſte propre ſygnyfycacyon worde becauſe hathe coactyue powre thyrde ſygnyfycacyon worde preeſte byſſhop euer aſmoche dothe rule ordre men accordynge lawe onely ſtate preſente lyfe althoughe lyfe come neyther graunted hym īmedyate maker lawe wyt chryſte punyſſhe man accordynge worlde therfore preeſte byſſhop called iudge properly thyrde ſygnyfycacyon whiche hathe coactyue powre neyther maye neyther ought punyſſhe man ſuche maner iudgement worlde eyther reale perſonall payne punyſſhement lyke maner doctour teacher operatyue phyſycyon comparyſon iudgement bodely helth men hauynge powre coactyue man haue ſayde aboute begynnynge preſent chapytre alſo ſentence ſaynt iohn̄ cryſoſtome playnlye openly agreynge mynde apoſtle fyrſte chapytre ſeconde epyſtle corynthyanes boke dyaloges whiche alſo entytled dygnytie preeſthode ſeconde boke thyrde chapytre ordre wordes haue brought heretofore vi parte v chapytre dyccion haue reherſed agayne cauſe ſhortneſſe theſe wordes whiche folowe nexte aforeſayde texte haue put theſe cauſe moch nede ſayth helpe crafte cōnynge men may perſwaded brought mynde whan ſycke theyr owne accorde frewyll offre ſelfe leche crafte phyſyke preeſtes onelye alſo preeſtes maye good gentle cured whether man chryſoſtome wolde ſtarte backe whan bounde verely thynge hath powre free lybertye ſhall make dyſeaſe worſe whether wyl refuſe wordꝭ whiche ſhulde haue done hym good ſtede ſurgeans ſalues inſtrumentes ioyneth addeth wounde vnto fyrſt wounde reaſon cōtempte occaſyon therof becōmed vnto hym ſelfe inſtrument peryllous deadely dyſeaſe man maye cure heale one agaynſt wyll ſayd chryſoſtome certayne wordes added hym conſernynge correccyon amendement people marked al curatꝭ cōſernynge ye cōpellynge cōſtraynīge ſayth theſe wordꝭ yf man led ye right fayth thā remayneth preeſt appertayneth charge vſe moch exhortacion moch wyſe dylygence moch pacyence may brynge man agayne nota faythe vyolence ſhall enforce hym ſelfe vttermoſte endeuoure perſwade ſuche perſone yt wyll retourne ryght fayth whiche hath fyrſt fallen lo howe holy man doth ſeperate departe iudgement preeſtes iudgement prynces gouernours becauſe coactyue iudgement neyther dothe belonge neyther ought belonge preeſtes aſſygnynge cauſes whiche haue ſayde oftentymes heretofore fyrſte becauſe coactyue power gyuen temporall lawe elles law maker prynce whiche graunted preeſtes chryſoſtomes tyme prouynce secondaryly yf ſuche coactyue power ſhuld graunted vnto euen ſo pyte graūted o• tyme wherein ſo many tyrauntꝭ clergye yet ſhulde vayne exercyſe vpon theyr ſubiectes ſpyrytuall thynge auayleth men compelled vnto neyther profyteth whyt eternall helthe ſayd ſame vpon texte ix luke yf man wylleth come lette hym denye hym ſelfe haue lefte ordre wordes partely becauſe theſe aforeſayd ſuffycyent partely cauſe ſhorteneſſe ſame alſo plyanely openlye mynde ſaynt hilarie conſtantius emperour whiche epyſtle amonge thynges thus wrote ſame emperoure god hath taughte knowlege hym ſelfe rather hathe exacted gettynge admyracyon hilarius eſtymacyon preceptes heuenly workes deſpyſed refuſed maner auctorytie coactyue men confeſſe knowlege hym ſelfe loo god wylleth men taughte knowynge confeſſyng hym wytte fayth man compelled therto deſpyſeth reherſeth ſame agayne longe ſayeng god requyreth coacte confeſſyon agayne afterwarde perſone preeſtes ſaythe thus receyue man excepte wyllynge hilarius man prayeng ſygne marke man hym profeſſeth therfore god wyll haue coacte confeſſyon owne ſelfe neyther wylleth man drawen therunto violence hym compulſyon wherfore ſame hilarius agaynſt auxentius byſſhop mylayne reputed arriane whiche procured men cō pelled force armes ſayde hilarius ſaythe confeſſe thoſe thynges feare hath bē yet many ſuch arrians yf myghte haue fulſwynge ſwerde theyr handes whiche belonged owne opynyon aboute rather agaynſt fayth rebukynge hym albeit ben ſo taughte thynge trouthe ſayth thus fyrſte maye petye laboure trauayle tyme age ſorowe bewayle folyſſhe opynyons theſe tymes whiche worldly thynges ſuppoſed beleued helpe defende god laboured ſeculare ambycyon defence mayntayne churche chryſte agayne ſame perſone ſame place ſayth ala pytie erthly helpes aydes cōmende fayth god cauſeth accepted chryſte proued without powre might whyles ambycion ioyned name church putteth men feare tyme punyſſhe hilarius rayleth agaynſte clargye banyſſhementes pryſons cōpelleth men gyue credence vnto ſhe beleued banyſſhementes pryſonamentes hilarius ſpeaketh churche vnderſtādynge colledge cōpany preeſtꝭ byſſhoppes mynyſters y• churche whome call cōmenlye clarkes alſo openly mynde ſaynt ambroſe valentiane ye emperour ſeconde epyſtle whiche intytled cōmune people whan ſayde ambroſe may wepe may ſory may mourne ſyghe agaynſt wepons armour agaynſt men warre agaynſt bothians teares wepons ſuche armoure preeſtes otherwyſe neyther ought neyther may reſyſte beholde preeſte ought althoughe myghte moue ſtereany wepon power coactyue agaynſt man neyther yet cōmaunde exorte wepons power coactyue moued namelye agaynſt chryſten men contrarye wherof worlde maye iudge thynke certayne preeſtes agaynſt doctryne holy ſcrypture ſayntes therfore accordynge trouthe open playne intencyon mynde apoſtle ſayntes whiche cheyfeſt doctours teacher churche faythe man worlde cōmaunded compelled ſpyrytualtie payne punyſſhement embracynge obſeruacyon preceptes lawe goſpell neyther infydell yet vninfydel wherfore mynyſtres lawe byſſhoppes preeſtes neyther maye iudge man worlde iudgement thyrde ſygnyfycacion neyther compell man obſerue preceptes goddes lawe namely without auctorytie humayne lawe maker ſuche maner iudgement accordynge lawe god ought exercyſed worlde execuſyon therof done onely worlde come wherfore xix mathewe iheſus ſayd vnto apoſtles ſuertye ſaye vnto whiche haue folowed regeneracyon whan ſone man ſhall ſytte ſeate maieſtye alſo ſhall ſytte vpon twelue ſeates iudgynge xii trybes iſraell maye ye ſe whan apoſtles ſhall ſytte chryſte iudges hym thyrde ſygnyfycacion verely worlde come world gloſe ſayth regeneracion ſay whan deed men ſhall ryſe incoruptyble wherfore mynde gloſe two regeneracyons fyrſte water holy ghoſt ſeconde generall reſurreccyon wherfore vpon theſe wordes alſo ſhall ſytte ſaythe gloſe mynde auguſtyne whan fourme ſeruaunte wytte chryſte whiche worlde iudged coactyue power dyd iudge ſhall exercyſe power iudge wytte reſurrection ſhall alſo iudges ¶ loo accordynge ſayeng chryſte goſpell expoſycion ſayntes chryſte hathe exercyſed iudicare power wytte coactyue power worlde rather beyng fourme ſeruaunt iudged ſuche maner iudgement alſo whan ſhal exercyſe ſuche iudicare power coactyue worlde apoſtles alſo ſhal ſytte hym iudge ſuche maner iudgement afore tyme byſſhoppes takevpon thē auctory tie chryſte ¶ wherfore hit worthely greatly meruayled wherfore byſſhop preeſte euer ſhulde take vpon wyll haue greatter auctorytie worlde chryſte apoſtles wolde haue fourme ſeruauntes haue ben iudged ſeculate worldly prynces ſucceſſoures preeſtes byſſhoppes onely refuſeth ſubiectes prynces contrarye example precepte chryſte obſtynat thomas caūterbury otherwyſe called thomas beket apoſtles alſo ſaye theym ſelues aboue prynces hygheſt power coactyue iuryſdyccion prynces ſubiectes vnto withſtondyng chryſte ſayd x mathewe ſhalbe ledde vnto kynges ruler ſake dyd ſay ſhall kyngꝭ ruler hit foloweth afterwarde ſame chapytre diſcyple aboue teacher bondeman aboue lorde therfore preeſt byſſhop yt ſuche one neyther may neyther ought exercyſe iudgemēt domynyon power gouernaunce coactyue world alſo euydently mynde aryſtotle iiii boke polytykes xii chapytre may proued alſo maner yf chryſt wylled preeſtes chryſte wold ye preeſtes newe lawe coactyue powre ye newe lawe iudgꝭ auctorytie ye ſame lawe iudge ment coactyue thyrd ſygnyfycacyon yt wyt defynynge determynynge contencyons debatefull actes men world ſuch maner ſentence doubteleſſe wolde haue gyuen ſuche ſpecyall preceptes ſuch maner thynges lawe lykewyſe dyd olde lawe moyſes whome god owne mouthe wordes man ordayned made gouernour coactyue iudge iewes red vii chapitre actes apoſtles cauſe alſo god gaue hym lawe thynges obſerued ſtate preſente lyfe contaynynge ſpecyally preceptes ſuch thynges departynge endynge contencions ſtryfes amonge men beynge moche lyke vnto lawe man touchynge ſome parte obſeruynge kepynge whiche preceptes men compelled conſtrayned worlde moyſes ſubſtytutes coactyue iudges payne punyſſhement preeſte appereth euydently xviii chapytre exodus chryſte hathe gyuen ſuche preceptes lawe goſpell ſuppoſed alredy gyuen ſhulde afterwarde gyuen lawes men whiche lawes cōmaunded obſerued alſo gouernours accordynge thoſe lawes obeyed euery ſoule leſtwyſe thoſe thynges whiche ſhuld cō trary lawe euerlaſtynge helthe therfore ſayth xxii mathewe xi marke gyue ceſare thoſe thynges belonge ceſare vnderſtandynge ceſare maner prynce gouernoure alſothe apoſtle xiii romaynes ſaythe greueth reherſe agayne let euery ſoule ſubiecte hygher powres alſo laſt chapytre fyrſte epyſtle timothe byddeth ſeruauntes obedyent theyr lordes ye thoughe infydeles gloſe alſo ſame place mynde auguſtyne agreeth ſame whiche haue brought afore ye viii parte v chapytre dyccyon auctoryties appereth euydently intencyon mynde chryſte apoſtle ſayntes al men ought ſubiecte obedyent lawes men thoſe iudges accordynge ſame lawes ¶ moreouer theſe aforeſayd thynges euydent chryſten men ye preceptꝭ ye olde lawe ar obſerued bounde obſerue kepe thyngꝭ olde lawe teſtament counſayled cōmaunded people iewes kepte obſeruacyon certayne thynges whiche cōmaunded iewes vtterly forbydden chryſten men example ſeremonyes vnder payne eternall perdycyon apoſtle teacheth iii vii chapytres romaynes ſeconde v galathianes ſeconde epheſyanes vii x chapitres hebrues whoſe mynde ſaynt ierome ſaynt auguſtyne agreynge ſay theyr epyſtles ſent one xi xiii concordynge eche obſeruers ſuche ceremonyes outher truely faynedly publyſſhynge lawe goſpel ſhal caſt downe ye dōgyon ye deuyl lykewyſe alſo chriſten men ar boūde ye obſeruacyon ye legales appereth ye apoſtle alſo auguſtine auguſtyne vpon yt ſayeng aforeſayd laſt chapitre timothe whan ſayd let chryſten ſeruauntꝭ requyre yt requyre whiche ſayde hebrues c aſmoche lawe grace preceptes ſpecyally gyuen cōtencyons debatefull actꝭ men worlde determyned ended lefte ſuch thynges ought determyned lawes men iudges accordynge thoſe lawes hauynge auctorytie humayue lawe maker prynce alſo certayne thynges lawe moyſes cōmaūded obſerued ſtate ye worlde come preceptes ſacryfyces certayne hoſtes oblacyōs made redempcyon ſynnes namely preuye ſynnes whiche cō mytted inwarde actes iudgement accomplyſſhynge preceptes man compelled conſtrayned payne punyſſhement preſent worlde lyke vnto theſe al counſeyles preceptꝭ newe lawe becauſe chryſte neyther wolde neyther cōmaunded man cōpelled obſeruacyon worlde albeit dothe cōmaunde generall cōmaundement ordynaunces mennes lawes ſhulde obſerued yet vnder payne punyſſhement done vnto tranſgreſſours worlde hym wherfore tranſgreſſours breaket mannes lawe yea punyſſhed world prynce maner moſt parte treſpaſſeth agaynſt lawe god contrary wyſe many actes doth leueth vndone treſpaſſeth agaynſte lawe god whiche cōmaundeth ſuche thynges wherof gyue cōmaundement lawes men vayne dedes whiche haue called inwarde actes neuer braſtynge forth whiche proued man hym yet hyd vnknowen god therfore lawe god conuenyently gyuen ſuche thynges duely done lefte vndone goodnes men preſente worlde alſo world come ¶ peraduenture ſome man wyll reken imperfeccyon doctryne goſpell yf haue ſayde contencyons debatefull actes men ſuffycyently ruled ſtate ſtate preſent lyfe let v ſaye doctryne lawe goſpell ſuffycyent lyfe euerlaſtynge goſpell ſuffycyentlye dyrected thynges done thynges auoyded eſchewed preſent lyfe ſtate world come eyther gettynge euerlaſtynge lyfe ye auoydynge eſcapynge euerlaſtynge punyſſhement whiche endes purpoſes ſcrypture made worldly reducynge contentious dedes men vnto equalytie dewe cōmenſuracyon concernynge ſtate ſuffycyencie preſent lyfe chryſte came worlde rule ſtrayghten ſuche maner dedes preſent lyfe onely lyfe come therfore rule temporall worldly actes men ben ſondry maners dyuerſe facyons dyrectynge vnto theſe endes one ſaye lawe god teacheth wyſe ought ſtryue go law aſke owne agayne afore iudge albeit doth forbyd therfore gyueth ſpecyall preceptes ſuche thynges haue ſayd afore rule theſe actes dedes wyt lawe man teacheth theſe thynges cōmaundeth tranſgreſſours punyſſhed wherfore xii luke whan certayne man deſyred chryſte worldly temporall iudgement betwene hym brother chryſt made anſwere thou man hath ordayned iudge deuyder betwene c yf ſayde come exercyſe ſuch temporall iudgement wherfore gloſe ſayth dothe vouche ſaue iudge ſutes ſtryffes lawe iudge vmpere worldly goodꝭ ſubſtaunces whiche hath iudgement bothe quycke deed arbytrement therfore actes dedes men coulde ſufficyently meaſured ruled lawe god euangelycall lawe ende preſente worlde dede cōmenſuratyue rule ſuche dedes proporcyon men lawfully deſyre ye ſtate preſent lyfe ben taught ſame lawe ſuppoſed eyther gyuen elles gyuen taughte lawes men without alſo defaulte lacke iuſtice myght chaunce throughe occaſyon contencyon men fyghtynge ſeperacyon departynge inſuffycyencie mannes lyfe world thynge maner men hate auoyde naturally ſayd therfore accordynge trouthe lawe doctryne goſpell vnperfyte ordayned apte haue ye perfeccyon worldly mater made gyuen īmedyatlye ſhulde dyrected cōcernynge thoſe thynges thoſe thynges whiche belonge obtaynynge gettynge ye ſe y• lacke neceſſary vnwryten vanytyes verity wolde ſaye ye ſcrypture perfite ſuffycient auctoure affyrmeth euerlaſtynge ſaluacyon auoydynge euerlaſtynge myſery whiche thynges ſuffycyent perfyte made determynynge cyuyle contencyous buſynes mater appertaynynge ende whiche men deſyre lawfully worldly lyfe truely yf ſhulde called vnperfyte therfore myght called conuenyentlye vnperfyte taughte hele bodelye dyſeaſes meaſure quantyties ſayle occyan ſee howbeit maye graunted ſafely vtterly perfyte ſo thynge perfyte onely one wytte god ſentence beynge vndoubtedly true gloſe mynde gregory beareth wytneſſe vpon ſyxte chapytre fyrſte epyſtle corynthyanes ſaythe ſay rebuke ſhame ſayth onely god perfyte gregory ſhulde examyne erthly cauſes haue gotten wyſdome exteryour thynges thoſe whiche endewed ſpyrytuall gyftes ought gregory wrapped entangled erthlye buſyneſſe nowe yf vnderſtande wyſdome exteryour thynges erthly cauſes contencyons holy ſcrypture wolde haue ſayde afterwarde whiche induced ſpyrytuall gyftes ſaye holy ſcrypture ought entangled erthlye buſyneſſes neyther wolde haue ſeperated ſuche perſones accordyng doctryne one moreouer becauſe apoſtle alſo ſayntes one expoſycyon afore called whiche ſuche know lege wyſdome wytte exteryoure thynges contemptyble perſones churche whiche thynge neyther apoſtle neyther yet ſayntes expoundynge wordes meaned thought lerned holy ſcrypture thus many maner legale actes men lawes alſo iudges howe whan whome ruled made ſtrayghte amended ſuppoſe haue ſhewed ſuffycyentlye intencyon purpoſed v ¶ coactyue iudge heretykes wytte whome appertayneth iudge world punyſſhe perſonall reall punyſſhementes whome whoſe vſe behole theſe ought applyed put vnto x chapytre bvt theſe thynges haue ſayd doubted cauſe yf inflyccyon exaccyon real perſonal paynes coactyue iudgement perſons coarted punyſſhed preſent lyfe apꝑteyneth onely hym heed gouernoure prynce hathe ben ſhewed tofore foloweth coactyue iudgement heretykes otherwyſe infydels ſcyſmatykes inflyccyon exaccyon applycacyon reall perſonall punyſſhement ſhall appertayne ſuche prynce gouernour whiche ſemeth appereth great inconuenyent aſmoche appereth belonge al vnto one ſame auctoryte knowe obieccyons iudge correcte offence treſpaſſe belongeth preeſte byſſhop dyſſerne cryme hereſye none ſhall appere counſayle coactyue iudgement correccyon cryme ſhall appertayne belonge preeſt byſſhop alone moreouer iudgement treſpaſſer exaccyon punyſſhemēt ſemeth appertayne hym agaynſt whome whoſe lawe treſpaſſer hath offended onely preeſte preſte mynyſtre goddes lawes byſſhop mynyſter iudge lawe god agaynſt whiche lawe pryncypally heretyke ſcyſmatyke otherwyſe infydell doth offende treſpaſſe whether company el ſynguler perſone foloweth therfore yt iudgement belongeth preeſte wyſe ſeculer gouernour appereth openly mynde ſaynt ambroſe fyrſt epyſtle anſwere obieccyōs proponed ualentian emperoure becauſe appereth ſemeth meaneth ſame throughout hole proceſſe ye ſame epyſtle haue lefte wordes becauſe breuytie ſhortneſſe ¶ let v ſaye ſoeuer treſpaſſeth offendeth agaynſt lawe god iudged corrected punyſſhed accordynge ſame lawe wchynge lawe ſo haſty captious thynke yt becauſe theſe word thauctoure wolde haue hereſy punyſſhed may ſeme reade litle ſe cōcluſyon wold haue punyſſhed ye cōmen law ſpyrytuall lawe man two maner iudges one iudge thyrde ſygnyfycacyon hauynge coactyue powre coarte tranſgreſſours lawe exacte punyſſhemēt onely one wyt chryſte haue ſhewed chapytre afore gone auctorytie iames iiii chapytre whiche iudge hathe wylled ordayned tranſgreſſours lawe ſhalbe iudged coactyue iudgement worlde come coatted payne punyſſhement onely worlde hath ſuffycyently appered ye chapytre afore gone iudge touchynge lawe preeſte byſſhop iudge thyrde ſygnyfycacyon ſo belongeth hym compell tranſgreſſoure lawe worlde requyre exacte payne punyſſhement vpon hym powre coactyue hath ben openly ſhewed v chapytre dyccyon laſt chapytre afore gone auctorytie apoſtle ſayntes inuyncyble reaſon yet notwithſtandynge iudge fyrſt ſygnyfycacyon whome apperteyneth teache exhorte rebuke reproue ſynners tranſgreſſours ſame lawe put feare drede iudgemēt eternall dāpnacion inflyccion euerlaſtynge payne whiche ſhal done coactyue iudge wyt chryſte world come haue declared y• vi vii chapytres dyccion wher treated powre keyes gyuen preeſtes alſo laſt chapytre afore compared preeſtes whiche lech phyſycions heretykꝭ taughte exhorted preeſte ſoules vnto bodely phyſycyons ſaynt auguſtyne ſayd auctorytie ye prophete mayſter ſentence recyteth iiii boke y• ſentences xviii dyſtynccion ix chapytre aſmoch heretyke ſcyſmatyke infydell ſoeuer tranſgreſſoure euangelycall lawe yf ſhall contynue cryme offence ſhal punyſſhed iudge whome belongeth punyſſhe tranſgreſſours goddes lawe ſuche one whan ſhal exercyſe iudyciarie powre iudge onely chryſt ſhal iudge auycke deed thoſe ſhall dye yet worlde come great mercy hathe graunted ſynners maye repent penaunce euen vntyll theyr laſt departynge paſſage world wyt euen vntyldeth iudge wyt paſtor curate byſſhop preeſte taughte exhorted preſent worlde ſynner reproued rebuked put feare drede iudgement eternal glorye euerlaſtynge dampnacyon come compelled wyſe euydent y• chapytre laſt afore gone yf ſhal prohybyted lawe man heretyke otherwyſe infydell ſhall contynue abyde heretykes punyſſhed whome remayne regyon ſoeuer ſhal founde regyon ſuch permytted heretykes ſede iewes nowe lawes men euen tymes chryſten people chryſten prynces chryſten byſſhoppes ſay lawfull man iudge heretyke myſbeleuer compell hym payne punyſſhement eyther reall perſonall ſtate preſent lyfe cauſe generall hereof man though ſynneth neuer ſo greatly agaynſt maner dyſcyplynes ſpeculatyue practyue punyſſhed coarted worlde precyſelye ſuche one ſynneth agaynſt cōmaundement lawe man yf prohybyted lawe man dronken make ſell noughtie leather ſhoes ſo yll wrought man may wylleth practyſe falſe phiſyke falſely teache exercyſe occupacions euen lyſte hym ſelfe dronkarde ſoeuer dyd amyſſe workes occupacyons wyſe ſhuld punyſſhed therfore ought marke take hede euery certayne ordre dewe pceſſe obſerued ye bultyng forth treuth maner coactyue iudgement world afore ſentence delyueraunce condempnacyon pronounced gyuen forth cōcernynge iuſt tryall truthe certayne thyngs enquyred ordre one whether worde dede wherof perſone accuſed ſuche ſayde knowe afore whiche ſayd cōmytted ſeconde thynge requyred whether prohybyted lawe man ſuche thynge done thyrde whether perſone accuſed hathe cōmytted offence whiche layde charge inquyſycyon made theſe thyngs foloweth iudgement ſentence cōdempnacyon agaynſt perſone accuſed el abſolucion delyueraunce example let man accuſed howe heretykes examyned iudged heretyke el coūterfayter golden veſſells metall perſone ſo accuſed delyuered dāpned coactiue ſentēce y• iudge ought fyrſt inquyred whether worde dede layde charge heretycall elles secōdaryly ought ſerched whether ſaye thynge ſuch wyſe forbydden lawe man thyrdly whether ſuch cryme offence hath ben cōmytted hym whiche accuſed therof laſte theſe inquyſycyons duely made foloweth iudgement coactyue eyther abſolucyon el cōdempnacion concernynge fyrſt theſe iii thyngꝭ gouernour iudge ought certyfyed whiche lerned ſkylled eche maner ſcyence whome belongeth cōſydre quidditie nature yt ſayenge dede whiche layde charge perſone accuſed ſuch perſons ar iudges ſuche thyngꝭ fyrſt ſygnyfycacion haue ſayd ſecōde chapytre dyccion bounde knowe y• nature ſuche thyngꝭ whome auctorytie gyuen prynce gouernour teache practyſe worke ſuch thyngꝭ ought iudge betwene thyngꝭ borowed layde kepe lyke cyuyle actes prynce gouernoure gouernour boūde know ſuch thyngꝭ albeit yf lawe perfyte ought ſertyfyed nature wordꝭ ſayenges workes dedes teacher wytneſſes recordes theſe thyngꝭ done iudgement ſentence gyuen y• gouernour wytneſſes outher cōdēpnacion el abſolucyon delyueraūce payneor punyſſhemēt eyther exaccion relaxacion made ſame powre doth ſometyme wyttynglye ꝑmyt fornycacion caſe lawe ordayned ſuch enormyties neyther byſſhop preeſte dothe prohybyte neyther maye ought prohybyte coactyue powre heretyke treſpaſſeth agaynſt ye lawe god yf ſuch ſynne alſo prohybyted lawe man punyſſhed dothe offende heretykes ben punyſſhed treſpaſſe agaynſt lawe man precyſe pryncypall cauſe wherfore man punyſſhed payne punyſſhement preſent worlde cauſe preſent effecte cauſe muſte nedes cryme broſteth forth folowe cauſe abſent ye effecte muſt nedely away lykewyſe contrary ſyde treſpaſſeth agaynſt lawe man offence ſhall punyſſhed world yet doth offende agaynſt lawe man onely many thyngꝭ prohybyted lawe man ar permytted lawe god yf man pay home hath borowed tyme ſet appoynted eyther throught lacke habylytie y• reaſon fortune chaunce forgetfulnes ſyckeneſſe throughe impedyment lettynge ſhall punyſſhed ſaye ſhall punyſſhed worlde breakyng daye paymēt ſo yt paye wardes caſe yt myght kepe daye world coactyue iudge accordynge lawe god yet notwithſtandynge ryghtuouſlye punyſſhed worlde coactyue iudge accordynge ye lawe man therfore treſpaſſe offēde agaynſt lawe god pryncypall cauſe neceſſary cauſe wherfore one ſhall punyſſhed worlde cauſe neceſſaryly foloweth effecte wyt payne punyſſhement ſtate ſtate worlde come cauſe fayleth fayleth alſo ſayd effecte ¶ therfore iudgement coartynge exactynge temporall payne punyſſhement prynce yf ſuch maner offence prohybyted lawe man cōmytte ſuch offence ought wyſe punyſſhed yt haue ſayd may proued declared famylyare exāple put caſe forbydden lawe man perſons infecte leprye ſhulded well abyde amonge cytezens myght phyſycion leche alone iudge theyr ſyckeneſſe accordyng facultie ſcyēce wytte whether full leprye coactyue powre owne auctorytie becauſe doctour phyſyke dryue whome ſhall iudge iudgemēt fyrſt ſygnyfycacion full leprye felowſhyp cōpany men c euydent vndoubted myght ſo thynge belongeth onely hym whome coſtume humayne lawe coactyue cōmytted wyt ye gouernour lawfull people cōpany pryuatefy iudge coarte punyſſhe man onely cheyfe gouernour whiche gouernour al cōcernynge crymes treſpaſſes offence wherof man accuſed cōcernyyge nature ſame accordynge determynacion lawe yf ſpeake thynge doubteleſſe ſhal yf perfyte lawe el owne wyſdome yf ſpoken lefte lawe ought vſe gyue credence iudgement lerned men ſuche well ſkylled artes ſcyences whiche treate nature ſuche workes dedes wordes iudgement phyſycyon concernynge perſons whiche full leprye ſo iudgemēt dyuyne ſynners fygured ſygnyfyed leprouſe perſons holy ſcrypture expoſycion ſayntꝭ lykewyſe alſo ought beleue ye iudgemēt goldſmyth synners fygured lepres cōcernynge deceytfull counterfaytynge golden cuppes metallꝭ ſemblably maner lerned cōnynge man kyndes thyngꝭ maye done wrought phyſycyon ſoules yt wyt preeſt ought iudge heretykes infydels iudgement fyrſte ſygnyfycation wyt pronoūcynge declarynge worde god whiche ſayenge whiche dede heretycall whiche iudge ſuche perſones iudgement thyrde ſygnyfycacion dāpnynge abſoluynge temporall payne punyſſhement cōpell whiche ſhall dampned ſuffre ſuch payne punyſſhement applye paynes exacted theſe crymes yf reall aſ well paynes exacted requyred crymes offence accordynge determynacyon lawe man theſe thynges ſay belonge onely prynce gouernour deputie theſe thynges whiche haue ſayde ſcrypture beareth wytneſſe xxv chapytre actes apoſtles whan apoſtle accuſed iewes heretyke thoughe falſely wrongfully inquyſycyon deduccion applycacion determynacyon cauſe made fore iudge iudge iudge therunto ordayned apoynted auctorytie gouernour lykewyſe cōtenciōs cyuyle actes dedes maſtery aſſoyle reaſons obieccyons made cōtrary theſe determynacyons whan ſayde iudgement heretyke belongeth vnto hym iudge whome belōgeth knowe cryme hereſy dyſtynccyon made becauſe equyuocacyon manyfolde ſygnyfycacion worde iudge iudgement one ſygnyfycation theſe wordꝭ wyt fyrſt ye ꝓpoſycion aforeſayd true ſygnyfication anſwers obieccyons made word iudgemēt yt wyt y• thyrd ye ſayd ꝓpoſycion falſe therfore nothynge cōcluded agaynſt determynacion propoſycyon afore alledged obieccyon foloweth hym belongeth iudgement treſpaſſer exaccion payne applycacion y• ſame yf reall agaynſt whome whoſe lawe treſpaſſer doth offende whan ſayde afterwardes yt heretyke treſpaſſeth offendeth agaynſt lawe god graunted therfore ſhal iudged hym iudge thyrde ſygnyfycacion accordynge lawe wyt chryſt worlde excepte mannes lawe neyther preeſte neyther byſſhop ſuche maner iudge lawe god onely iudge fyrſt ſygnyfycacion teacher therof namely yf lawe cōpared men ſtate ſtate preeſte teacher prynce preſent lyfe agayne ye fyrſt propoſycyon ſyllogyſme ſuppoſed true ſence haue ſayd wyt yt iudgemēt trāſgreſſour apperteyneth hym coactyue iudge agaynſt whome agaynſt ye lawe wherof keper tranſgreſſour doth offende lawe meane laſt ſygnyfycation onely let v adde therunto ſeconde propoſycion beynge true heretyke treſpaſſeth onely agaynſt ſeculer iudge takynge worde thyrde ſygnyfycacyon agaynſte lawe wherof keper takynge worde lawe laſt propre ſygnyfycacion wytte coactyue onely agaynſt coactyue lawe iudge heretyke cō dempned preeſte worlde let v therfore cōclude heretyke iudged ſuch iudge coactyne iudgemēt worlde maker lawe ſo ordaynynge payne punyſſhemēt exacted ſame trāſgreſſour alſo ſame iudge payne yf real applyed ſame iudge hym whome tēporal law hath ordayned appoynted applyed elles muſt make dyſtyncion ye fyrſt propoſycion accordyng ye equocacion ye wordꝭ made parologiſme deceyptlull reaſon laſt afore inferred cōcluded thus neceſſyte ſome man cōdempned iudged heretyke world worlde coactyue iudgement really ꝑſonally wayes ergo iudged ſome preeſt byſſhop excepte ꝑaduenture iudgemēt y• fyrſt ſygnyfycacion neyther alſo foloweth therfore ergo carnal tēporal goodꝭ exacted heretyke cōdēpned punyſhemēt parte punyſſhemēt offence ought applied byſſhop preeſt lykewyſe doth alſo folowe man iudged coūterfayter money ergo iudged coyners excepte peraduēture iudgemēt y• fyrſt ſygnyfycation y• thyrde wyt coactyue iudgemēt neyther foloweth alſo tēporall goodes whiche exacted hym punyſſhemēt ought applyed ye vſe behoue coyners company ſynguler perſone oughte iudged coactyue iudgement gouernoure onely gooddes hym applied accordige ye determynacion ye humayne lawe ¶ obieccyon groūded vpon y• auctorytie ſaynt ambroſe se theſe obieccyōs begynnynge chapytre anſwered ſayd yt vnderſtode meaned y• heretyke cryme hereſye bolōgeth iudgemēt preeſtꝭ byſſhoppes takynge worde iudgemēt fyrſt ſygnyfacacion y• thyrde neuer byſſhop preeſt vſed ſuch maner iudgemēt coactyue owne auctoryte aboute ſtake prymytyue churche albeit afterwardes proceded vnto ſuche thyngꝭ occaſyon certayne graūtꝭ made pryncꝭ gouernours therfore ſo euer doth cōfydre begynnyngꝭ ſuch thyngꝭ thoſe thyngꝭ ſemen nowe longe abuſyon ſtrēgth haue face apparaūce ryght ſhall ſeme hym tryflynge phantaſyes dreames thus determyned iudge iudgement coactyue powre ouer infydels heretykes ¶ certayne ſygnes teſtymonyes example aſwell canonycall ſeculare ſcrypture whiche ſhewed true hath ben determyned ye iiii v viii ye ix ye x chapytres dyccyon concernynge ſtate byſſhoppes generally preeſtes wherfore chryſte hath ſeperated ſtate wyt ſtate pouertie ſtate prynces gouernours xj chapytre aſmoch hathe ben ſhewed v chapytres afore gone aſwell auctorytes holy ſcrypture certayne euydent polytycall cyuyle argumentes byſſhop preeſt clarke belongeth iuryſdyccyon coactyue perſone worlde nowe wyll declare ſame manyfeſt ſygnes alſo teſtymonyes whiche ſygnes one euydent rede neyther yt chryſte apoſtles dyd euer place inſtytute iudge deputye theyr ſtede vſe ſuch maner domynion execute ſuch maner iudgement albeit ſemeth lyke true apoſtles neyther ignoraunte neyther dyd lytle regarde whiche ſo neceſſary thynge ſocietie cōpanyeng men one worldly lyfe yf knowen thynge haue ben appertaynynge theyr offyce yf ben wyllynge ſhulde belonge theyr ſucceſſours wyt byſſhoppes preeſtꝭ wold haue gyuen ſome precepte el leaſte ſome coūſayle cōcernynge ſame touchinge inſtytutynge makynge ſpirituall mynyſtres byſſhops preeſtꝭ deacōs ſhewed taught forme maner howe ſhuld done thynge knowen ſuffycyently apper tayne vnto theyr offyce ſayenge ſaynt paule thyrde chapytre fyrſt epyſtle timothe fyrſt chapytre titus appereth alſo euydently many place ſcrypture ¶ chryſt hath ſeperated departed offyce preeſtꝭ byſſhops ye offyce pryncꝭ gouernours yf lyft myght haue exercyſed ye eſtate prynce offyce preeſte togyther haue ordayned apoſtles lykewyſe haue done ye ſame wolde ſo rather thynge conuenyent hath ordayned al thyngꝭ beſt wyſe yt myght wolde yt theſe offyces ſhuld ſondry maners facyōs alſo executed ſondry maner perſons aſmoch come teach hūblenes deſpyſynge world beynge way wherby myght obtayne euerlaſtynge helth ye entēt therfore chryſte teacher humblenes pouertie myght teache humylyte deſpyſynge worlde temporall thyngꝭ example taught doctryne came world moſt lowe humble maner vtter refuſynge ſuch temporal thyngꝭ becauſe knewe men nothynge leſſe moche taughte worke enſāple wordes preachynge wherfore seneca ſayth ix epyſtle loke ſayth ought done lerned y• doer chryſte wolde borne moſt lowe vyle maner pouertie greatteſt deſpiſynge world teache v practyſe ye ſame thyngꝭ exāple wherfore red ſeconde chapytre luke blyſſed vyrgyn mother wrapped hym courſe clothes ſhe layde hym downe y• mawnger beholde poorely borne mannes houſe beholde layde downe mawnger cratche place beaſtꝭ fed lyke true yt wrapped cloutꝭ borowed another body becauſe ioſeph blyſſed virgyn ſtraūgers pylgrymes paſſengers yt place whiche thus borne pouertie lyued alſo pouertie growen age wherfore ſpeakynge owne pouerte viii mathewe ix luke ſayde fox haue dennes byrdes ayre haue neſtꝭ ſone man hath place maye laye downe heed ſtate beynge ſtate pfeccion al preceptes counſayles duely accordyngly obſerued fulfylled taught electe choſe thoſe whiche wyll mynde dyſcyples cheyfe folowers namely ſucceſſours yt ſame offyce exercyſynge wherof came worlde wherfore xix mathewe x marke biſſhoppes ought choſe xviii luke certayne man demaūded queſtyon hym ſayenge wyſe good mayſtre thynge ſhal obtayne get euerlaſtynge lyfe iheſus anſwered hym ſayd knoweſt thou cōmaūdemētꝭ thou ſhalte kyll thou ſhalte thefte c ſayde agayne haue obſerued kepte theſe youth iheſus herde yt ſayde hym yet thou lackeſt one thynge red mathewe yf thou wylte perfecte go ſell thou haſte gyue poore folkes thou ſhalt haue treaſure heuen agayne xiiii ſame luke ſayde dyſciples ſoeuer dothe renoūce al thyngꝭ poſſeſſeth dyſcyple lo yt ſtate pouertie deſpyſynge ye world beſemeth euery ꝑfecte man namely dyſciple chryſt ſucceſſour ye paſtoral offyce yea moreouer ſtate maner neceſſary hym ought coūſayle exhorte vnto deſpyſynge y• world yf intende purpoſe yt profyte good ſhal growe teachynge preachynge yf ſuche maner ꝑſone doth poſſeſſe ryches deſyreth domynyōs ſoueraygneties teacheth men vnto whome ſpeaketh deſpyſe theſe thyngꝭ perſone verely owne workynge doynge doth manyfeſtly reproue rebuke owne preachīge wordes wherfore chriſoſtome agaynſt ſuche preacher boke compunccyon herte ſayth wyſe ſay onely lucre chryſoſtome aduaūtage alſo moche loſſe hynderaunce verely great cō dēpnacion hym ordereth wel trimeth ſpeache regardeth nothīge maner lyuynge ſame alſo y• mynde ariſtotle fyrſt rhapytre x boke etykes ſayth thus wordꝭ dyſagreynge ye workꝭ hym yt ſpeaketh whiche workes ſene perceyuyd bodely ſences ſayd workes deſtroye trouth yt whiche ordereth trīmeth wordes ſo well beleued ſayth lytle ye wordes agreynge vnto workꝭ dedꝭ ſhal beleued therfore chryſt whiche knewe howe thyngꝭ done moſt cōuenyently wyllynge credence gyuen vnto wordes wherby taught cōtempte world deſpyſynge eſchewynge worldly vanyties carnall pleaſures counſayled yt workes ſhulde cōformable wordes doctryne wherfore v mathewe ſayth ſhulde wardꝭ doctours teacher ſuch thyngꝭ perſone apoſtles let lyght yt wyt doctryne whiche cōpared lyghte ſo ſhyne men yt maye ſe good workꝭ gloſe ſayth theſe wordꝭ requyre workꝭ yt may ſene ſo reaſon doctryne may confyrmed eſtablyſſhed workes requyred preeſte el lytle credence gyuen wordes doctryne workꝭ ſene wherfore y• gloſe vpon texte x mathewe poſſeſſe golde ſyluer c ſhewynge y• cauſe hereof ſayth wyſe yf theſe thynges wyt golde ſyluer c myght ſeme preache becauſe ſoule helthe cauſe lucre aduauntage teacher paſtours men poſſeſſynge ſuche thyngꝭ rather deſtroy fayth deuocyon men theyr cōtrary workes exāples ſtrength eſtableſſhe theyr wordes doctryne becauſe ſet theyr owne workes dedes manyfeſtly agaynſt theyr owne teachynge workꝭ men take hede rather wordes greatly feared leaſt laſt throughe lewde exā ples theyr workes brynge chryſten people deſperacyon euyll lyfe byſſhoppes world come ſuch exāples workes maner mynyſters churche bothe byſſhpps preeſtꝭ clarkes cōſequently moſte euydently ſytteth vpon greateſt trones chayers ye churche ſay whiche moſt hyghe rowmes auctorytie ſeme note well thynge beleue ſhall iudgement god done worlde let tel beſeche cōſcyence towardes god yf beleue ſhall made ryghtwyſe iudgemēt god ye worl • come done ye moſt parte pope rome theyr cardynalles preeſtꝭ byſſhoppes whiche made ouerſeers put truſte take charge ſoules dyſtrybute tēporalles churche poore folke alſo maner preeſtes robbe poore people deacon clarkes euery ſorte accordynge theyr powre ſay thefte robery ſuche tēporall goodes whiche haue ben ordayned bequeſt deuoute chryſten men ſuſtētacion preacher goddes worde theyr poore folke eyther delyuer whyles lyuynge el bequeth dyenge great ſūmes money may y• poore nedy people theyr nere kynſfolke ſoeuer robbynge wherof man doubteth poore men ſame goodes let tell alſo requyre cōſcyence accordynge chryſten relygyon preeſte waſte vnthryſtely goodes poore men lyuynge tēporally carnal facyon theyr mynyſtrynge goſpell ought cōtented meate drynke clothes couer mynde apoſtle laſt chapytre fyrſte epyſtle timothe cōſume waſte goodes apperteynynge ye poore people ſo many ſuperfluous vnneceſſary thyngꝭ horſes ſeruaūtes feaſtes bankettꝭ vanytes pleaſures open ſecrete great incōuenyences enormytes whiche done cōcernynge dyſtrybucyon eccleſiaſtical offyces benefycꝭ euyl vnhappely beſtowed clargy benefycꝭ paſſe ouer many thoſe offycꝭ eyther moch prayer intreaty obtayne fauour ſeculer men beynge ryche great powre money whiche offred yf laufull ſpeake dyſtrybuters ſelues elles mynyſtres symon magus interceſſours broker ar gyuen ignoraunte ſclaunderfull perſones chyldren ſtraū gers symon magus vnknowen hatefull euydently vnlerned perſons iudgemēt whole cōmen people albeit yet yt apoſtle thyrde chapytre fyrſt epyſtle timothe dothe teache eccleſiaſticall offycers ought knowen honeſt perfecte men lyfe maners alſo doctryne lernynge wherfore ſayth yt place yt wyt byſſhop preeſte ought haue good reporte teſtimony euen without church moche whiche within churche lytle afterwardes ſame chapytre ſayth deacon lykewyſe ought chaſte let theſe alſo proued tryed fyrſt afterwarde let ſo mynyſtre man may accuſe ſome may ſay cōuenyently moſt parte well proued world knoweth wyt howe moch money able gyue howe great intreatīge prayer able make becauſe wyll take inhande nombre reken vp pertyculerly inconuenyences maner impoſſyble harde makyng generall ſūme actes workes preeſtꝭ deacōs well nyght al mynyſtres temple wytnes chryſt callynge vpon ourſelues note this▪ beare well awaye iudgement condempnacyon yf make lye yt aforeſayd byſſhoppes welnere nowe dayes worke maner contrary thynges thoſe whiche teache vnto men obſerued accordynge doctryne goſpel togyther inflamed deſyre pleaſures vanytyes temporall tranſytory goodes worldly domynyons dygnytes laboure enforcemēt ryght bothe pryuy open wronge go aboute purchace gette ſuche thynges vyolentlye poſſeſſeth whiche thynges euery one chryſte apoſtles trewe folowers dyd theyrſelues deſpyſe alſo taught cōmaunded deſpyſe namely moſt al thoſe preeſtꝭ ſhuld ye deſpiſers worldly thynges whiche ought preache deſpyſynge worldly thynges vnto men chryſte yf wolde yf ſene perceyuyd expedyent preacher myght haue kepte eſtate prynce ruler worlde haue ſuffered paſſyon lykewyſe ſame ſtate fledde ſyghte mountayne refuſe deſpyſe ſuche maner ſtate teache deſpyſed haue alledged fore iiii chapytre parte vi iohn̄ ſemely accordynge whiche teacheth preacheth deſpyſynge ſuche maner ſtate bere ſame eſtate rather beare ſtate ſubiectes lowe vyle perſones whiche maner ſtate bothe chryſte hymſelfe alſo apoſtles kepte whyles world contrarywyſe ſtate outwarde pouertie lowe vyle ſtate ſemely cōuenyent prynce gouernour ſuche ſtate expedyent hym ſtate good ſubiectes may haue reuerence euyll ſubiectꝭ may pouertye ſettynge ſemely prynce muſt nedes ryght hyghe eſtate powre rycheſſe feare drede whiche eſtate alſo yf nede ſhall requyre may able punyſſhe rebellyons tranſgreſſours lawes whiche thynge coulde conuenyently yf poore lowe ſtate whiche cauſe alſo offyce preacher cōuenyent ſemely hym yf prynce gouernoure ouer people ſhulde counſayle exhorte men ſtate pouertie humble lowe ſtate agayne yf man ſtrycken one cheke ſhulde holde cheke ſtryker alſo hym whiche taketh away cote ought gyue alſo gowne rather go lawe ſtryue iudge hym hathe wronged v men wolde lyghtly gyue credence hym ſuche thyngꝭ ſtate whiche ſettynge ſemely hym whiche dothe alſo beare ſhulde clene contrary owne wordes teachynge beſydes ſhuld alſo vnconuenyently vnaccordynglye asmoche apperteyneth offyce reſtrayne hold vnder punyſſhement yt done iniury wrōge yet albeit yt requyre haue ſuffred iniury wrōge yf ſhuld preache yt iniuryes forgyuen ye doer ſhulde gyue euyl men certayne occaſyon largely treſpaſſynge doynge euyll alſo ye ꝑſones offended haue ſuffred iniury wrōge ſhulde gyue occaſyon doubte myſtruſte obtaynīge true iuſtice cauſe chryſte hath ordayned al thīgꝭ alwayes y• beſt wyſe maner wold ye offycꝭ pryncꝭ gouernours preeſtꝭ ioyned togyther one ꝑſone rather deꝑted y• one ye executed dyuerſe ꝑſons ſemeth expreſſely mynde ſaynt barnarde iiii chapytre bernarde ſeconde boke wrote eugenius pope de conſideratiōe ſayth thus dareſt thou whiche arte lord vſurpe take vpon offyce apoſtle thou arte apoſtolyque perſone take vnto domynyon lordſhyppe playnely thou arte forbydden bothe yf thou wylte haue bothe togyther one tyme thou ſhalte loſe elles ſuppoſe reken thou arte excepted nombre whome god complayneth wyſe haue reygned haue ben prynces gouernours haue knowen theſe reherſed thyngꝭ beareth wytneſſe decree certayne hyſtoryes byſſhopps rome donacyon cōſtantyne founde wryten certayne donacion pryuylege whiche alſo approued alowed ſame conſtantyne emperoure romaynes wherby graunted ſaynt sylueſter men ſaye iuryſdyccyon coactyue temporall domynyon coulde emperour iuſtly ſoueraygnete ouer church al preeſtꝭ byſſhoppes worlde aſmoche euery pope rome hym alſo ye congregacyon company preeſtes byſſhoppes confeſſe knowlege graunte valure ſtrength conſequently muſt alſo graūt ſame conſtantyne fyrſt iuriſdyccyon powre vpon namely ſeynge ſuche maner iuryſdyccyon knowen belonge vnto ouer clarke laye man vertue wordes holy ſcrpture whiche ſaynt barnarde ſayth expreſſely eugenius boke conſyderacyon barnarde iiii chapytre ſayth thus peter knowen haue come forth tyme eyther adourned precyous ſtones ſylke garmentes couered gold caryed whyte palfray lyke ye barnarde lordes hauynge thycke garde men warre aboute hym thoughe none theſe thynges yet beleued myght well ynoughe fulfyll holſome charge whiche gyuen hym yf thou doeſt loue fede ſhepe theſe ſeculer pompes powres thou arte ſucceſſour peter pope ſucceſſoure cōſtātyne peter conſtantyne thus conclude offyce prynces gouernours none offyce ſemely mete preeſtꝭ ſuche one contrary wyſe offyce preeſte ſemely prynces ye dyfference let haue nothynge paule toke nothynge peter ſaye added nothynge wherin euydent inferyor ſeynge made ſo perfyte lord god thynge whiche ye cōferrynge preachynge theyr owne myght adde perfeccion lo paule paule ſent pryncypallye peter peter apoſtles chryſte īmedyatlye whiche thynge apoſtle largelye expreſſynge fyrſt chapytre ſame epyſtle ſayth thus paule apoſtle men man iheſus chryſte god ye father gloſe ſayth mynde ambroſe paule apoſtle electe ſent men wyt ananias ambroſe paule ſent ananias certayne men ſayd men certayne elected ſent apoſtles lytle foloweth ſame gloſe alter mynde auguſtyne apoſtles ſemed greatter becauſe afore apoſtle ſemed leaſte becauſe laſte hereof appereth worſhypfull becauſe fyrſt apoſtles made ordayned chryſte beynge yet partlye man ſaye mortall laſt apoſtle wyt paule conſtituted made chryſte nowe beynge whole god paule worthy apoſtle ſaye vtterly mortall god father whiche dyd wrought ſame myght open declare wherfore ſayd neyther man ſayth afterward hath rayſed hym vp deathe ſo hath worthelye worſhypfullye made chryſte beynge īmortall dyd chryſt beynge mortal agayne apoſtle cōfyrmynge afterwarde ye ſame chapytre ſayth thus gyue knowlege wyt brethern goſpell whiche hath ben preached man haue receyued learned man reuelacyon iheſu chryſte gloſe mynde auguſtyne ſayth wytte bretherne goſpell whiche hath ben preached mynde man teachynge verely man haue receyued neyther learned man ſo man dyd electe preache inioyne preache neyther learned man teachynge reuelacyon ieſu chryſte lo neyther peter neyther ye apoſtles man hath choſen paule ſent hym inioyned hym mynyſtery preachynge goſpell ſame iudged alſo ye apoſtles peter therfore powre moche leſſe coactyue iuryſdyccion god īmedyately vpon ye apoſtles neyther īſtytutige ye offyce preeſthode neyther ſegregate departe ſondre ſende offyce preachynge ſauynge onely maye ſafelye graunted peter afore aboue howe maner peter ſuperyor apoſtles age aūcyentnes perauenture afore offyce touchynge abydynge rome dyd receyue al gentile wyllynge conuerted dyd preache goſpel playne open ſpecyally byſſhop rome becauſe dyd exercyſe offyce paſtore byſſhop hauynge y• auctorite therof chryſt cōmaūdement reuelacion conſent apoſtles eleccion touchyng ſaynt peter whome ſeconde purpoſes ſayde ſhall proued appere saynt peter onelye byſſhop rome alſo neuer cam euydently ſaye proued holy ſcrypture byſſhop rome neyther yet greatter thynge euer rome ſemeth wonderful thynge yf ſhuld ſo red certayne cōmune eccleſiaſticall legende ſayntꝭ peter dyd come rome fore ſaynt paule dyd preache worde god afterwarde taken moreouer afterwarde ſaynt paule cōmynge rome peter togyther ſo many conflyctꝭ dyſputacyons symon inchaūter togyther ſtroue ſo greatly fayth agaynſt emperours theyr mynyſters laſt accordynge ſame hyſtorye bothe beynge headed togyther cōfeſſyon chryſte dyed lorde ſo dyd cōſecrate y• churche rome chryſte ſay wonderful thynge yt neyther ſaynt luke whiche wrote actes apoſtles neyther ſaynt paule made mencyon ſaynt peter ¶ agayne ſaynt peter came rome afore great lykelyhode beleuyd wryten laſt chapytre actꝭ whan paule ſpake vnto ye iewes fyrſte cōmynge amōge thynges wyllynge ſhewe cauſe cōmynge rome ſaythe iewes cryed cōtrary conſtrayned appele vnto ceaſer ſayd vnto hym neyther receyued letter cōcernynge iewry neyther cam ye brother ſhewed ſpake harme deſyre thy mynde opynyon touchynge ſecte knowe euery ſayd agaynſt let therfore ſercher trouthe ſechynge cōtende ſtryue onely tell whether probable lykely man ſaynt peter came rome afore paule dyd ſhewe nothynge fayth chryſte whiche iewes ſpekynge paule called ſecte furthermore paule rebukynge theyr īcredulyte hardnes beleue yf knowen peter ben preached coulde yt wolde haue ſayd brought hym wytnes buſynes whiche wytnes reſurreccyon chryſt open thyrde actes agayne haue ſpoken alredy wyll ſuppoſe thynke yt paule beynge abydynge rome two yeres neuer cōuerſacion cōmunycacyon cōpanye felowſhyp peter yf luke wolde haue made mencion therof whiche wrote hyſtory actes leſſe famouſe place whan paule founde peter made mencyon hym cōuerſaunt hym corynthe rede fyrſte epyſtle thyrde ye corynthyās antioche ſecōde ye galatiās ſo many place yf therfore foūde hym rome could wolde haue named hym rome beynge y• moſt famous cytie y• foreſayd hyſtory ſaynt pet er ruler byſſhop therof theſe thynges maner vnbeleueable wherfore ſemeth hyſtorye legende prouable ſuſtayned holden poynt ought counted amonge ſcryptures whiche called apocriphe legenda eccleſiaſtica canonycall veryte holy ſcrypture holden vndoubtedly ſaynt paule byſſhop rome yf hym rome yet paule ſyngulerly pryncypally byſſhop rome cauſes aforeſayd ſaynt peter byſſhop antioche appereth ſeconde chapytre galatian byſſhop rome ſay agaynſt lykelyhode holde peter dyd preuent com paule rather cōtrary wyſe paule preuented peter thynge whiche moſt taken hede marked pryncypall purpoſe yt albeit ſome congruence reaſon myght appere whiche called whiche waye ſoeuer ſpecyally ſucceſſours ſaynt peter namely epyſcopall ſee rome worſhypful reuerēde ſucceſſours apoſtles yet neceſſyte holy ſcrypture cauſeth v beleue ſucceſſours apoſtles ſubiectes ye ſame ſucceſſours peter power auctorytes aforeſayd thoughe graunted apoſtles vnegall auctoryte yet peter therfore apoſtle vertue wordes ſcrypture powre vpon ye inſtytute depoſe neyther touchynge dygnyte preeſthode haue called eſſencyall dygnyte neyther touchynge ſendynge determynynge appoyntynge certayne place people neyther interpretynge ſcrypture catholicall fayth neyther touchynge coactyue iuryſdyccyon man world wherfore neceſſyte ſemeth folowe neyther ſucceſſour ſyngularly ſpecyallye ſoeuer maner ſo called hath aboueſayde maners powre vpon ſucceſſours may euydently confermed auctoryte ſaynt iherome brought epyſtle euādre aboute ende chapytre laſt aforegone ¶ auctoryte inſtytutynge byſſhoppes whome dothe appertayne belonge alſo inſtytutynge curate mynyſters churche touchynge dignytꝭ offycꝭ ſeperable vnſeperable xvij chapytre thus haue ſhewed effectyue cauſe ſay inſtituter ordayner y• fyrſt auctoryte belongynge preeſtꝭ haue called eſſencyall auctoryte nowe reſteth remayneth vnto v determyne ſpeake auctoryte whiche ſome preeſtꝭ preferred ſome ruler outher certayne preeſtꝭ certayne people bothe certayne prouynce place moreouer ho wherby belongeth ſame dyſpence ordre dyſtrybute certayne tēporall thyngꝭ called benefyces churche aagayne alſo howe meane coactyue iuryſdycciōs hath come certayne perſone alſo ꝑſones maner moſt cōuenyently belōgeth determyne y• doubtfull ſences holy ſcrypture namely cheyfly thoſe thyngꝭ appertaynynge neceſſyte ſoule helthe whan theſe thyngꝭ ſhall one ſuffycyently opened declared thynge ſhall euydentlye appere whiche pryncypally intended purpoſed v euer ſyns begynnynge worke ¶ yet afore proſecute thynges purpoſed partyculerlye expedyent neceſſarye ſhewe fyrſt maner inſtytucion determynynge aſſygnynge byſſhops preeſtes vſed aboute ſtate begynynge prymatyue churche whiche thynges aboue ben afterwardes deryued begynnynge theſe thyngꝭ taken chryſte heed ſtone wherupon catholyke churche groūded accordynge chryſt ſtone vpon ye church grounded buylded ſayenge ſaynt paule iiii v epheſianes x fyrſte coryntheanes certayne gloſe alſo ſayth ſame xvi mathewe vpon texte upon ſtone wyll buylde churche heed ſaye ſtone foundacyon churche wyt chryſte gaue preeſthode apoſtles epiſcopall auctoryte ouer vpon nacyons people determynynge appoyntynge ſeuerallye ſo vnto certayne place people yt myght laufull euery one preache ſoeuer albeit ſome deputed aſſygned preache amonge gentyles ſome preache amonge iewes ordynacyon amonge themſelues elles holy ghoſt whiche thynge alſo ſemeth mynde gloſe ſeconde galathians vpon texte whan knowen grace gyuen amonge gentyles c ſayth gloſe chryſt gaue paule ſhulde mynyſtre gentyles peter ſhulde mynyſtre iewes yet dyſpenſacyon mynyſterye goſpell ſo dyſtrybuted departed betwene two bothe peter myght preache gentyles yf cauſe ben paule alſo iewes ſame alſo paule ſemeth haue meaned lykewyſe xi romaynes whan ſayde ſhall put mynyſterye honoure yf maye meane prouoke nacyon emulacyon folowynge nacyon calleth iewes whome came carnall generacyon gloſe ſayth ſame place whiche wordes apoſtle ſemeth thought iudged yt ſame powre one inſtytuted made preeſt hath powre mynyſtre euery indyfferentlye vpon euery people albeit certayne ordynacyon man ſome determyned aſſygned one certayne place people another namely nowe adayes theſe thynges ſemeth conſonaūt agreable ſcrypture alſo reaſon chryſte gyuynge euery one apoſtles generall admynyſtracyon xxviii mathewe ſayde indyfferently go therfore teache nacyons aſſygnynge appoyntynge none determynate place people ſeme otherwhyles haue ben determyned aſſygned ſome ſpecyall nacyon people reuelacyon god aſmoch apoſtle ſayth hymſelfe xxii actes chaunced whan retourned iheruſalem prayenge temple rauyſſhed mynde ſe hym wyt chryſte ſayenge vnto make haſte go quyckely iheruſalem ſhall receyue thy teſtymonye thou ſhalte bere lytle foloweth chryſte ſayd vnto hym go thy way ſhall ſende nacions farre hence lo ſemeth paule ſomtyme reuelacyon aſſygned ſome determynate certayne place people beſyde alſo apoſtles receyued ſame aſſygnemente certayne ordynacyon man wherfore ſayde ſeconde galathyans thus iames peter iohn̄ gaue barnabas ryght handes ſocietie felowſhyp ſhuld preache amonge gentyles amonge iewes lo determynacyon aſſygnemēt apoſtles vnto certayne people determynat prouynces made īmedyatlye ordynacyon man vndoubted ſuche determynacyon aſſygnement made īmedyatlye reuelacyon god ordynacyon amonge themſelues dyd receyue perfeccyon holy ghoſt whiche ¶ ſame alſo ſayde agreable reaſon caſe put byſſhop curate beynge aſſygned appoynted certayne prouynce people gone forthe ye prouynce cōmytted hym ſe chaunce adayes ofte nedefull conuenyent dyd mete ſome chaū ce elles purpoſe ſome infydell baptyſed yet deſyrynge hymſelfe ſome perſone ſayde curate baptyſed made chryſtened yf ſayde curate baptyſe hym kepynge forme ſacrament vndoubted man verely truely baptyſed albeit peraduenture dothe ſynne deedly whiche doth ſo baptyſe man prouynce ſubiected cōmytted hym wherfore maye conclude man determyned aſſygned epiſcopall ſacerdotale powre haue called eſſencial powre vnto certayne place people powre indyfferentlye concerneth nacyons people yet ſuche determynacyons aſſygnementes haue ben made ſomtyme dyuyne reuelacyon prymatyue churche often ordynacyon man namely nowe adayes cauſe auoydynge ſclaunder occaſyon offence amōge byſſhoppes preeſtes one euydent cō modytes profytes whiche ſhall aſſygne hereafter ¶ theſe thynges thus premyſed put nowe cōmynge pertycularely ſpecyally thynges purpoſed begynnynge chapytre fyrſt ſhall ſhewe ſuche determynat inſtytucyon apoſtles certayne people prouynces moſte cōuenyent cauſe effectyue imediat reuelacion chryſt el y• able ordynacion amōge themſelues afterwardes ſhall ſhewe imedyate cauſe effectyue determynate inſtytucyon theyr fyrſt ſucceſſours afore conuercion people expreſſe wyll apoſtles el many yf el many preſent togyther one place prouynce whiche neceſſarye ordayne inſtytute preeſt byſſhop elles onely one apoſtles accordynge dyſpoſycion place people tyme laſte ſhall ſhewe dethe apoſtles theyr abſence ſecondarye inſtytucion byſſhops ſpyrytuall mynyſters mynyſtres churche moſt conuenyent manere poſſyble conuerſacyon man done vnyuerſyte hole congregacion multytude chryſten people place prouynce ouer whiche ſayde byſſhoppes mynyſtres ought inſtytuted ordayned rather pertyculare cōpanye perſone ſo afterwarde thynges ſhall ſhewed cōſequētly ¶ fyrſte therfore theſe maye appere wytte conuenyent cauſe aſſygned aforeſayd determynacion apoſtles certayue place c deuyne reuelacyon ye conuenyent delyberacion amonge themſelues moche neyther theſe two ſemeth erroure malyce haue chaunced come betwene deuyne reuelacyon man doubteth eleccyon made apoſtles ſemeth probable beleued inſpyred holye ghoſt haue alledged tofore xx chapytre iohn̄ ¶ furthermore ſay ſecondary inſtytucyon determynacyon aſſygnement theyr fyrſt ſucceſſours namely afore conuerſyon people imedyate cauſe effectyue doer ought many apoſtles ſome one alone maner aforeſayd yf togyther many elles one alone founde place proued fyrſt ſcrypture rede vi actes apoſtles dyd maner inſtytucyon deacon yea touchynge fyrſte eſſencyall call inſtytucion ſayde ſame chapytre ſette theſe men vnderſtande thou whiche made deacon afore ſyght apoſtles wyt apoſtles makynge theyr prayer layde theyr handes vpon dyd bryng peter alone brought afore ſyght apoſtles neyther peter alone toke vpon hym auctoryte apoſtles peter onelye layde handes vpon yt ſhulde made deacon ſeuerally put handes vpon apoſtles dyd put handes alſo agreable reaſon lyke trewe many apoſtles togyther toke ſure councell dyd leſſe erre aboute perſone promoted outher preeſthode holy ordre one taken ſeuerally hymſelfe alledged afore laſt chapytre cauſe aſſembled ſenyours preeſtes determyne doubte aboute lawe goſpell facte worke cyrcū cyſyon agayne cōmune aſſente taken awaye mater occaſyon offence contencyon whiche lykelyhode ſhulde haue ryſen amonge yf one preſence wold haue taken vnto hym powre ſuperyoryte aboue whiche contencyon ryſen amonges euen chryſtes tyme chryſte determyned ended ſhewynge expreſſynge y• equalyte haue tofore alledged xxii mathewe xxii luke alſo haue ſhewed largely by▪ ye apoſtle alſo expoſycyons ſayntes chapytre laſt afore gone moreouer moſt reſonable ſo therby myght take away preſūpcyon ſuche ſyngularyte theyr ſucceſſours alſo gyue example doynge lykewyſe ſhall ſhewed hereafter ix parte hereof gloſe vpon vi chapytre actes ¶ yf togyther elles many place nedefull make byſſhop ouerſeer gouernour ſome multytude chryſten men kepynge fayth ſayde verely fooles deſire promocyon dygnyte albeit yt ye prymatyue churche ſomtyme happened ye byſſhop choſen ye multytude becauſe ther lacked chryſten prynces rule matter yet yt daūgerous maner author ſayth ful wel moche daungerous nowe adayes wyſe way nowe alſo one byſſhop electe yf men might ſure ye byſſhops apoſtles complexcion becauſe great doubte yt thāked god wyſe ſure way founde yt eleccyon togyther belō geth kyngꝭ moſte gracyous hyghenes one alone myght lawfully thige namely ſmall multytude chryſten people ſame rude vnſkylled dyſcerne perſone moſte conuenyent offyce byſſhop ouerſeer cheyfelye many ſuffycyent able perſons ſayde offyce whiche thynge chaunced often tymes paule fyrſte ſucceſſours appereth ſuffycyentlye actes apoſtles owne epyſtles vnto timothe tite ſuche maner inſtytucion myght lawfully ought made one alone maye proued therby choſen beſte moſt conuenyent paſtor outher lawfull eche one owne pleaſure make hymſelfe ouerſeer vnto mynyſterye goſpell el thynge ought done eleccion multytude beynge ſubiecte elles ſome apoſtles beynge prſente fyrſt waye ſlaundre erroure myght haue chaunced ſlaundre offence ſaye yf two perſons mo wolde haue taken auctoryte vnto erroure alſo inſuffyciencie vnablenes paſtor lykewyſe moſt cōmunely fooles ambicious perſons deſyreth goeth aboute take vpon dygnyties prelacy vertuoſe wyſemen ſeconde way wyt yf prelate ſhulde haue ben made eleccyon multytude erroure inſuffyciencie perſone promoted myght lykelyhode haue chaū ced reaſon ſayd multytude weke bothe nombre alſo knowlege rude ignoraunt begynnynge mayne prouyncꝭ namely iewrye eaſye begyled appereth holy epyſtle galatian many epyſtles wherfore apoſtle thyrde fyrſte epyſtle coryntheās ſayth thus brother myght ſpeke ſpyrytuall perſones carnall perſones chyldren babe chryſte gaue mylke drynke yet able ſtronge neyther yet able ſtronge yet carnall wherfore conclude ſure wyſe way inſtytucion ſhulde done ye eleccion determynacion aſſygnemēt one apoſtles whoſe lyfe wyſdom wayghtye greatter reaſon holy ghoſt lyfe wyſdome ſuch multytude albeit denyed expedyent apoſtle haue aſked counſayle multytude touchynge maners conuerſacion perſone whiche preferred elected ſayd offyce ¶ nowe conſequentlye premyſſes wyll ſhewe tyme apoſtles holy father ſuccedynge nexte apoſtles office namely cōmunytes congregacions chryſten men beynge one perfyte īmedyat factyue cauſe doer inſtytucion aſſygnacion gouernour ouerſeer whether greatter nowe call byſſhop whether ſmaller whome nowe call curate preeſt hauynge cure alſo inferyor mynyſtres ought hym ſayd multytude hathe graunted auctoryte make ſuche inſtytucyons eleccyons ſame auctoryte belongeth laufullye put depryue euery one ſayd offycers ſuche maner offyces compell eche one exercyſe execute offyce yf thought expedyēt neceſſary yet ought marke take hede yt althoughe powre preeſte euer ſo exhybyte mynyſterie maye put hādes vpon men indyfferently promote hym preeſthode hym ſelfe beynge graū ted o• moſt gracyous ſorayne forde ye kynge acte ꝑlyament mynyſtre preparynge god abſolutlye īmedyatlie gyuynge powre preeſthode yet ſay al yt laufull hym gyue euery maner man pleaſure neyther goddes lawe mannes lawe ye cōmunytes chryſten men beynge nowe perfyte ſayde ouer yf exhibyte ſayde mynyſterye crymynous ſclaunderous ꝑſone otherwyſe inſuffycient vnable treſpaſſeth worthy punyſſhement agaynſt law god man alſo doth ſynne punyſſheable moche tedyous kyngꝭ grace troubeled owne perſone eleccion euery ſymple preeſte mē cal therfore grace may cō myt yt offyce yt ben vndernethe hym whiche yf wolde neglegēt vncircūſpecte leccyon yet ought byſſhop haſtely put handes vpon ſhew ye kyng therof onely remedy againſt ye lawe god appereth apoſtle thyrde fyrſt epyſtle timothe fyrſte chapytre tite byſſhop ought faulteles mete qualytyes property rekened vp ſame elles moche lyke thought ſuppoſed deacon wherfore place afore alledgyd vnto timothe ſayth deacon lykewyſe oughte chaſte c dothe alſo ſynne treſpaſſe worthy payne agaynſt lawe man promotynge inſuffycient vnable perſone eccleſiaſticall ordre appereth theſe thynges haue ben ſhewed viii chapytre dyccion cōmytteth outwarde acte tournynge noyaūce hurte man ſtate preſent worlde alſo worlde come whiche maye proued hym dede althoughe wolde ſaye naye promotynge vnto cōmune offyce ſuche perſone whiche maye corrupte lyfe maners bothe men woman el ſo moche expedyent neceſſarye bothe ſtate preſēt worlde alſo worlde come faſcion maners men ſuche one euer leude euyll dyſpoſed otherwyſe inſuffycient vnable ¶ theſe premyſſes wyll forthermore inferre conclude neceſſyte cōmunyties chryſten men beynge nowe perfyte belōgeth onely kynge deputy haue ouerſyght electe determyne aſſygne preſente perſones whiche promoted eccleſiaſticall ordres perſones therfore promoted vnto eccleſiaſticall ordres approued dyſalowed ſentence iudgement hym whiche cheyfe hygheſt gouernour ſame auctoryte ſayd perſones alſo inſtytuted remoued cure offyce byſſhop preeſte prohibited excercyſynge therof alſo yf malycyouſe purpoſe dyd ceaſe excercyſe theyr offyce cōpelled excerciſynge doynge theyr dutye lefte throughe theyr lewdnes man myght fall ieopardy eternall death lacke baptiſme ſacrament verely vnderſtanded cōmunyties chryſten men whiche alredy perfyte ſuch place prynce gouernoure hethen prynce moſte parte cōmunytes well nere cōmunytes aboute ſtate tyme prymatyue churche approbacyon reprobacyon chaſt matrymony meaneth perſones promoted eccleſiaſticall ordres aforeſayd inſtytucions auctorite prohybyte exercyſe theyr offyces compell ſame ſhulde appertayne belonge preeſt byſſhoppe wyſe parte chryſten multytude beynge ſayd place hym alone yf alone without conſent knowledge ye myniſter ye churche choſen gouernoure cheyfe ruler ſuche maner promotynge inſtytucyon prelate curate faythe holſome doctryne chryſte
