actes defence iniurye ſhall neyther iniurye man neyther man theym ſtate ſtate preſent worlde offyce prynce hyghe gouernoure none parte membre cōmunyte hath ben ſhewed xv fyrſt dyccyon alſo apoſtle expreſſed xiii chapytre romaynes haue brought wordes v chapytre dyccyon ſame alſo mened v chapytre fyrſt epyſtle tymothe whan ſayde beſeche therfore obſecracyons made fyrſt kynges hyghe auctoryte may leade quyete peaceable lyfe lykewyſe agayne parte prynce dependeth hath nede accyon operacyon preeſte preeſte receaueth doctryne ſacramentes dyſpoſynge men worlde remouynge puttynge awaye ſuche thynges contrarye ſaluacyon eternall beatytude ſtate worlde come yet dyfferently dyuerſe maner worke receaue theſe operacyons eche prynce beynge coactyue iudge worlde ordynacyon god maye lawefully exercyſe impreſſe operacyon coactyue power doynge ponyſſhement vpon preeſte yea thoughe wyllynge contente yf hathe ben tranſgreſſor lawe man whiche contrary lawe god hath ben ſhewed proued v viii chapytres dyccyon xv fyrſte dyccyon byſſoppe preeſte becauſe accordynge lawe god coactyue iudge man worlde hathe ben ſhewed xv fyrſte dyccyon iiii v ix dyccyon iudge fyrſte ſygnyfycacyon worde iudge operatyue teacher leche phyſycyon operacyon precepte compell man neyther ought compell man payne ponyſſhement outher reall perſonall touchyng preſent lyfe fyrſt propoſycyon ſayd argumentacyon falſe wherin ſayde ſoeuer thynge worketh perfyte operacyon ought touchynge iuryſdyccyon vnder thynge worketh leſſe perfyte inconuenyent abſurdytye operacyon propoſycyon aforeſayde propoſycyons ioyned vnto foloweth neceſſarely manyfeſte inconuenyent falſe propoſycyon wytte ſpeculatyue dortor leſtewyſe hygheſt pryncypall phyloſopher metaphyſycyon vnder iuryſdyccyon prynce gouernoure accordynge lawe man moche none practyue habytes ſcyences qualytes beſydes faythe prynce gouernoure el man neyther operacyon procedynge brought forth ſayde habytes ſcyences egall perfeccyon habyte ſcyence methaphyſycyon accyon operacyon brought forthe whiche habyte operacyon maye chaunce prynce gouernoure lacke afterwardes obiected ſemeth inconuenyent vnſemely thynge byſſhoppe rome elles byſſhoppe ought vnder coactyue iudgemente hym prynce worldly gouernoure anſwered ſayde none conuenyent byſſhoppe vnder ſame lyke iudge vnder lorde mayſter ſayde byſſhop owne fre wyll hath determyned cōuenyent ordynacyon ordre worlde obſerued chryſte whiche bothe god man wyllynglye ſubmytted hymſelfe coactyue iudgement ponce pilate whiche vycare deputye hym emperoure ſo alſo dyd holye apoſtles taught alſo ſame accordyngly vnto lawe god hath ben playnlye euydently ſhewed ſcrypture ſaynges ſayntes doctours iiii v dyccyon hathe ben alſo repeted reherced agayne xxviii ſame dyccyon wherfore alſo moche ſeruaunte greatter mayſter neyther apoſtle greatter hathe ſent hym haue alledged brought ſcrypture ſayinge bernarde xxviii chapytre dyccyon bernarde amonge thynges ſaythe thus fyrſte booke v chapytre de conſideratione vnto eugenius ſeruaunte thanne mynyſſher dygnyte yf wylleth greatter lorde mayſter dyſcyple yf wylleth greatter ſente hym ſone yf wyll goo beyonde termes boundes whiche forefather haue ſette mayſter lorde ſayd hath made ordayned iudge ſhall iniurye ſeruaunte dyſcyple excepte maye iudge men inconuenyent verye conuenyente alſo neceſſarye quyetnes tranquyllyte cyuylytye cōmune weale byſſhop preeſte clerke vnder coactyue iudgemente prynces ſeculer gouernoures contrarye hereof vtterlye inconuenyent intollerable furthermore becauſe byſſhoppe rome byſſhoppe vycare chryſte mynyſter exercyſe maner offyce world onely touchynge certayne determynate offyce example touchynge preeſthode whiche offyce ſuche one regarded conſydered coactyue iudgemente neyther ſuperyoure inferyour touchynge ſuche iudgemente alledged openlye wordes aryſtotle viii parte ix chapytre dyccyon prynce ſeculer gouernoure prynce ye vycare god vycare mynyſter god touchynge offyce prynce gouernoure whiche offyce conſydered regarded ſuperyour inferyour ſubiecte touchynge coactyue power wherfore xiii romaynes apoſtle exceptynge none preeſtes byſſhoppes ſaythe let euery ſoule ſubiecte hyghe power putteth cauſe hereof forth ſaynge mynyſter god se nowe howe prynce vycare god vyolent coactyue euyl men world therfore foloweth ponyſſher wroth vnto hym yt euyldoer ſo byſſhop preeſt may euyldoer neyther chryſt neyther apoſtle hath aſſygned tyme iudge outher theyr worke example el theyr wordes hath ben ſhewed dyccyon place afore alledged obieccyon whiche put forthe maner coucluſyon ſayde yf ſhulde expedyent neceſſary correcte prynces obieccyon gouernoures whan ſhall treſpace offende agaynſt goddes lawe mā ne lawe ſemeth maye conuenyently corrected aſmoch haue ſuperyor cyuyle regymente leſtwyſe pryncypall hygheſt therfore ought vnder coactyue iudgemente preeſtes byſſhoppes anſwered ſayde prynce gouernoure offendynge treaſpaſſynge agaynſt lawe god man anſwere howe prynce gouernoure corrected may ought corrected conuenyently eccleſyaſtycall mynyſter byſſhoppe preeſte wordes exortacyon increpacyon rebukynge yet ſobre dyſcrete meſurable maner accordynge doctryne apoſtle ſeconde alſo iiii chapytre ſeconde epyſtle tymothe expoſycyon chryſoſtome whiche haue brought heretofore ix chapytre dyccyon wyſe coactyue power auctoryte ſuche maner power dothe appertayne preeſte byſſhoppe ſuche one vpon man worlde hathe ben oftentymes proued repeted heretofore touchynge reaſon whiche fynallye added touchynge iuryſdyccyon ſuperyor vnto emperoure another obieccyon rome maye ryghte inſtytute depoſe ſayde emperoure whiche hathe tranſlated empyre greekes vnto germaynes perſon great cherles hathe ben ſayd made tranſlacyon pope rome ergo pope ſuperyor emperour may ryghte inſtytute depoſe emperour anſwered ſayde yf fyrſt propoſycyon argument taken indefynytly vnyuerſally anſwere ye ſecond propoſycyon nothyng inferred cōcluded moch ſyllogyſme may made indefynyte propoſycyon partyculer propoſycion yf taken vnyuerſally ſo ſayd euery tranſlator romayne empyre grekes vnto germaynes ſuperyor tranſlacyon mayne empyre emperour c excepte ſubiecte propoſycyon wyt tranſlator empyre c determyned propoſycyon myght proued falſe many true reaſons yf man īvery dede yet ryght tranſlated empyre elles yf done owne power power man gyuen vnto hym vnto proctour deputye perſon ſaye whiche ſo tranſlated empyre ſhulde therfore hym ſelfe alone haue ſuperyor iuryſdyccyon vnto emperoure neyther ryghtfull power auctoryte inſtytute depoſe hym yf aforeſayde propoſycyon determyned euery mortall man whiche hath tranſlated maye iuſtlye ryghtfully tranſlate romayne empyre greekes vnto germaynes owne propre auctoryte graunted hym perſon ſuperyor coactyue iuryſdyccyon emperour rome maye ryghtfullye inſtytute depoſe hym propoſycyon ſo graunted ſeconde propoſycyon whiche ioyned vnto byſſoppe pope rome whiche hath trāſlated empyre hath ben ſayde denyed vtterly falſe contrary propoſycyon hath ben proued xv fyrſt dyccyon alſo contrarye concluſyon whiche inferred hath ben certyfyed ſurely proued ſcrypture ſaynges ſayntes catholyke doctours iiii v chapytres dyccyon hathe ben repeted reherced agayne verye many place thus hath ben obſerued dede without reclamacyon grudge olde father paſtores byſſhoppes rome thus haue gone throughe doubtes moued thyrde xxvii chapytres dyccyon lette ſuffycyente thus make ende queſtyones pryncypallye purpoſed intended v worke ¶ thus endeth ſeconde dyccyon boke ¶ thyrde dyccyon parte worke entytled defender peace whiche table two fyrſte dyccyons ¶ reherſall callyng remembraunce agayne thynges pryncypally intended determyned fyrſte ſeconde dyccyon certayne ſequele neceſſary folowynge whiche thynges ſhalbe ſpoken boke haue vnto thynges whiche haue ben ſayd dyccyons aforegoynge fyrſte chapytre moche dyccyons aforegoyng haue aſſygned marked forthe ſynguler ſpecyall cauſe nowe cyuyle dyſcorde intranquyllyte vnquyetnes certayne realmes certayne cōmunytes whiche ſame thyng ſhall alſo hereafter cauſe debate ſtryfe cōmunytes excepte letted ſtopped tymes wytte exiſtymacion opynyon deſyre enforcement whiche byſſhoppe rome companye clergye ſyngulerlye eſpecyally laboure poſſeſſe ſeculer domynyons temporall thynges ſuperfluouſlye whiche domynyons ſouereygntes ſayde byſſhoppe endeuoureth chalenge hygheſt vnto hym ſelfe tytle full power whiche pryncypallye graūted hym ſayth chryſt perſon ſaynt peter haue ſayde laſte chapytre fyrſt dyccyon hath ben reaſonable cauſe repeted oftentymes reherſed verye many chapytres declaracyons holy interpretours therof many proued doctours teacher ſame afterwardes alſo vi vii chapytres ſeconde dyccyon haue ſcryptures certayne reaſons aſſygned ſhewed howe great thynges power auctoryte preeſtes byſſhoppes whome ſome one haue ſhewed xxiiii chapytre ſame ſuche fulnes power dothe belonge neyther ioyntlye ſeuerally whiche fulnes taken ſelues vſurped namely byſſhoppe rome reaſon whiche thynges ſo v declared ſhewed ſemeth appereth rote ſynguler malygnyty ofte named prohemy preface ſuffycyently cut vp wherfore nowe ye braunches twygges graffes dyſcorde ſtryfe whiche peſtylence myſchefe hath brought hetherto yea ceſſeth yet dayly brynge realmes cōmunytes maye y• ſooner drye vp able hereafter haue yſſue ofſprynge ſprede ſhall ii dyccyons aforegone brynge forth ye thyrde dyccyon whiche remayneth behynd whiche dyccyon ſhalbe nothynge elles neceſſarye playne clere euydent inferryng certayne conclucyons folowyng ye thyngꝭ afore wryten beyng outher euidently knowen lawfull alwayes hym ſuter ſtryueth lawe appele coactyue iudgement whiche hathe ben graunted byſſhoppe preeſte hym prynce gouernoure ¶ xxviii concluſyon ¶ multytude ſynguler perſon goſpell mynyſtred proued xv fyrſte viii ſeconde ¶ xxx concluſyon ¶ conclucyons bothe verye many nombre alſo verye profytable myght inferred whiche neceſſyte foloweth determynacyons made two fyrſte dyccyons partes yet notwithſtandynge tyme wyll holde v contented theſe whiche haue redy deduced moche gyue eaſye ſuffycyent entraunce occaſyon reder geather inferre ſuche lyke mo ſuffycyent alſo cuttynge awaye aforeſayde great myſcheyfe otherwyſe called byſſhoppe rome alſo cauſe therof ¶ ende thyrde dyccyon parte worke whiche called defender peace ¶ peroracyon concluſyon worke reader thou haſte moſt gentyll reader worke whiche albeit perauenture ſet forth paynted wordes eloquent ſpeache yet wyſdome dyſpyſed ſayde worke hathe lyked pleaſed auctor therof entytle defenſor pacis ſaye englyſſhe defender maynteyner
